[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/start-guide#installing-plus-ai)

Installing Plus AI


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use Plus AI in Google Slides or PowerPoint (or both!)

Install the Google Workspace add-on or PowerPoint add-in and then login with your Plus account to get started.

# PowerPoint version requirements | Plus Guide

The Plus AI add-in for PowerPoint uses Powerpoint API 1.5, so unfortunately some older versions of PowerPoint are not supported.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint/powerpoint-version-requirements#supported-versions)

Supported versions

Plus AI requires the following versions of PowerPoint

*   **Mac:** Version 16.64 (22080400)
    
*   **Windows:** Version 2208 (Build 15601.20230)
    
*   **Windows:** Perpetual Volume License Office 2021 - Not supported
    
*   **iPad:** Not supported
    

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint/powerpoint-version-requirements#what-version-of-office-am-i-using)

What version of Office am I using?

Refer to this Microsoft help article: [https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/office/about-office-what-version-of-office-am-i-using-932788b8-a3ce-44bf-bb09-e334518b8b19](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/office/about-office-what-version-of-office-am-i-using-932788b8-a3ce-44bf-bb09-e334518b8b19)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint/powerpoint-version-requirements#what-can-i-do-if-i-want-to-use-plus-ai-but-cant-upgrade-my-microsoft-office)

What can I do if I want to use Plus AI but can't upgrade my Microsoft Office?

Unfortunately we don't have a great workaround solution for you at the moment in PowerPoint.

You can always install [Plus AI in Google Slides](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides)
 instead and export your Google Slide presentation as a .pptx file. (Google Slides is free to use).

[PreviousInstall in PowerPoint](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint)
[NextPowerPoint desktop app recommended](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint/powerpoint-desktop-app-recommended)

Last updated 9 months ago

# Install in Google Slides | Plus Guide

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides#id-1.-get-the-plus-ai-add-on)

1\. Get the Plus AI add-on


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Install the Plus add-on: [https://workspace.google.com/marketplace/app/plus/214277172452](https://workspace.google.com/marketplace/app/plus/214277172452)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides#id-2.-open-google-slides-or-google-docs)

2\. Open Google Slides or Google Docs


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides#google-slides)

Google Slides:

In Google Slides, create a new presentation or open an existing one. Here is a shortcut to create a new presentation: [http://slides.new](http://slides.new/)

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides#google-docs)

Google Docs:

In Google Docs, create a new document or open an existing one. Here's a shortcut to create a new document: [http://docs.new](http://docs.new/)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides#launch-in-slides)

3\. Launch the Plus AI add-on


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In Google Slides or Docs, go to the **Extensions** menu, click **Plus AI**.

In Google Slides, Select **New presentation** to generate new slides from scratch or **Edit with Plus AI** to insert, remix, or rewrite slides.

In Google Docs, Select **Edit with Plus AI** to generate or edit content.

Login with the Google account you want to use with Plus.

Don't see any options in the Extensions menu (except "Help"?). This is a common Google Slides bug. Reload the page in your browser or open a new presentation and try again.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FMIv0nvJh2KZxHPrcoR7e%252FCleanShot%25202023-07-03%2520at%252014.43.02%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43087599-a61d-4988-a35a-3005af5f8c3f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3cb1b2a4&sv=2)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides#id-4.-select-a-paid-plan-to-start-your-free-trial)

4\. Select a paid plan to start your free trial


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You need a paid plan to use Plus AI. If you're a new customer to Plus, you can start a 7 day free trial. You'll need to add a credit card, but you can [cancel](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#manage-or-cancel-my-subscription)
 at any time during your trial.

Learn more about our plans [here](https://www.plusdocs.com/pricing)
, and more about [billing](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing)
 here.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides#id-5.-generate-a-new-presentation)

5\. Generate a new presentation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides#google-slides-1)

Google Slides

Enter a prompt, paste a document or article, or configure your presentation slide-by-slide.

Learn more about generating a presentation:

[Generate a presentation](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation)

Did you know you can also use Plus AI in Google Docs? [Learn more.](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-google-docs/generate-a-new-document)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fh4jKIsI9frSpaiVzDvTt%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.20.00%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e5d5a08-0148-499b-86b2-535b7e325a00&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c30746cb&sv=2)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides#get-started)

🪄 Get started!


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Click here](http://slides.new/)
 to open a new Google Slides presentation or [here](http://docs.new/)
 to open a Google Doc and get started with Plus AI.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Having issues? Here are some common issues and how to fix them.

[Troubleshooting](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting)

# Install in PowerPoint | Plus Guide

We strongly encourage that you use the **PowerPoint desktop app** (and not PowerPoint in your browser)

[Learn more](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint/powerpoint-desktop-app-recommended)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint#id-1.-get-the-plus-ai-add-in)

1\. Get the Plus AI add-in


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint#from-the-powerpoint-app-recommended)

From the PowerPoint app (recommended)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FDRGk3du3tf3jJ2IJwUej%252FInstall%2520Plus%2520AI%2520Slide%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2427ffb4-c074-4363-91bc-a96b57ed0d21&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=714df5da&sv=2)

Installing Plus AI in PowerPoint: Home > Add-ins > Search for Plus AI

*   Open your PowerPoint app
    
*   In the **Home** tab, click on **Add-ins** (in the right hand side of the menu).
    
*   Search for "Plus AI for PowerPoint" > Click **Add**.
    

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint#from-the-appsource-store)

From the AppSource Store

Alternatively, you can install the Plus add-in from the Microsoft AppSource Store: [https://appsource.microsoft.com/en-us/product/office/WA200007130](https://appsource.microsoft.com/en-us/product/office/WA200007130)

If you run into authentication issues, see troubleshooting section below. We recommend installing directly in your PowerPoint app instead (see above).

*   Click **Get it now** -> you may be prompted to sign in and confirm your account details.
    
*   You will then be prompted to open the add-in in your Plus app.
    
    ![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FdwDft5rZ2TUqGMThn1Yf%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-19%2520at%252012.58.51%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da128e4ba-0ffb-41f9-89eb-ccfdaf8c0207&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea59a121&sv=2)
    
*   In PowerPoint, click **Allow and Continue** to finish installation.
    
    ![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FNKObHE8SAKPVEcBBOR2T%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-19%2520at%252013.01.49%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D477c489c-6c3b-40bd-9c22-70766df17d23&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dbe80d5b&sv=2)
    

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint#id-2.-launch-plus-ai)

2\. Launch Plus AI


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint#from-the-home-tab)

From the Home tab

*   In your PowerPoint app, go to the **Home** tab, click on **Add-ins.**
    
*   Search for Plus AI if it doesn't show up immediately under My Add-ins
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F5I8hq5Odi9SmhlwkeeFG%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-13%2520at%252014.48.13%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44b1143f-3ff6-4997-b1fc-79be41aec12d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7cd26334&sv=2)

Launch Plus AI in PowerPoint: Go to Home > Add-ins. Search for Plus AI if it doesn't show up.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint#from-the-insert-tab)

From the Insert tab

Once Plus AI is installed, you can also find it directly in the **Home** tab

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FfyAYW3d9y7tZmoUvYW8K%252FCleanShot%25202025-06-30%2520at%252015.48.37%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D834fa46b-c007-4f24-8e7e-3170601fd76a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ac7bbef7&sv=2)

Launch Plus AI in PowerPoint from the Home tab

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint#id-3.-log-into-your-plus-account)

3\. Log into your Plus account


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Currently, we only support logging in with a Google account. If you need to use a different authentication method, [contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

Your Plus account is separate from your Microsoft account. You can sign up and use Plus AI with a Google email address even if you're logged into PowerPoint with a Microsoft account.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint#id-4.-start-your-trial)

4\. Start your trial


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You need a paid plan to use Plus AI. If you're a new customer to Plus, you can start a 7 day free trial. You'll need to add a credit card, but you can [cancel](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#manage-or-cancel-my-subscription)
 at any time during your trial.

Learn more about our plans [here](https://www.plusdocs.com/pricing)
, and more about [billing](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing)
 here.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint#id-5.-generate-a-new-presentation)

5\. Generate a new presentation


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on **\+ New Presentation** to open Plus AI.

Start from a prompt or upload a document to create a presentation. You can learn more about generating presentations below.

[Generate a presentation](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Need help with installation?

[Troubleshooting](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting)

# PowerPoint desktop app recommended | Plus Guide

We strongly encourage that you use Plus AI in the PowerPoint desktop app and not in your browser (Microsoft 365).

Some limitations of PowerPoint in your browser can cause major formatting issues, which also affect Plus AI-generated content.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint/powerpoint-desktop-app-recommended#how-to-switch-to-the-desktop-app)

How to switch to the desktop app

In PowerPoint in your browser, click on the **Editing** dropdown (top right of your screen) and click **Open in Desktop App.**

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FB2P52JKvwB6rxuQRBbAd%252FCleanShot%25202024-07-09%2520at%252020.51.24%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D21947f31-029d-4fdd-9f28-9b062fdea7d1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ddd9abf8&sv=2)

How to switch to working in the PowerPoint Desktop App

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint/powerpoint-desktop-app-recommended#how-to-install-the-powerpoint-desktop-app)

How to install the PowerPoint desktop app

Refer to the installation instructions from Microsoft:

[https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/office/download-and-install-or-reinstall-microsoft-365-or-office-2021-on-a-pc-or-mac-4414eaaf-0478-48be-9c42-23adc4716658#bkmk\_signintodownload](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/office/download-and-install-or-reinstall-microsoft-365-or-office-2021-on-a-pc-or-mac-4414eaaf-0478-48be-9c42-23adc4716658#bkmk_signintodownload)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint/powerpoint-desktop-app-recommended#known-issues-related-to-powerpoint-in-the-browser)

Known issues related to PowerPoint in the browser

These are some examples of problems that only affect the browser version of PowerPoint. Stick to the PowerPoint desktop app to avoid these!

*   Auto-resizing of text does not work for Plus AI generated slides, so you may have lots of overlapping text. You can edit the text box (e.g., add and delete a space at the end of each text block) to activate autoresizing.
    
*   Icon slides generated by Plus AI may not be formatted correctly.
    
*   Occasionally, AI generated images may be added to the wrong slide.
    
*   Occasionally, AI generated slides may only contain placeholder text.
    

[PreviousPowerPoint version requirements](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint/powerpoint-version-requirements)
[NextPlus AI plans and billing](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing)

# Prompt errors | Plus Guide

There are certain types of content that will not work with Plus AI. If you use these in your prompts, you'll get an error when trying to generate presentations and slides.

If you're getting an error related to a prompt, but it seems like we're getting it wrong, [let us know](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting/prompt-errors#content-moderation)

Content moderation

Certain types of content are not allowed with Plus AI, including:

*   Hate speech
    
*   Harassment
    
*   Self-harm
    
*   Sexual content
    
*   Violence
    

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting/prompt-errors#code)

Code

You cannot include code snippets in Plus AI prompts. If you need to include code in your presentation, use a prompt in plain English (or [other languages](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/languages)
) and then add your code snippets after the presentation has been generated.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting/prompt-errors#other-errors)

Other errors

The most common error when generating presentations and slides is that Plus AI takes too long to respnd (or runs into some other kind of error). Most of the time, retrying the request will work.

If you continuously run into errors when generating presentations, [let us know](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

[PreviousTroubleshooting](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting)
[NextGenerate a presentation](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation)

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

# Plus AI for teams | Plus Guide

Invite and manage members of your team in Plus AI to share the benefits of your subscription.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-for-teams#what-are-teams-in-plus-ai)

What are teams in Plus AI


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Plus AI paid features are shared across teams. If you have any paid plan, all members of your team will have access to those benefits, like unlimited presentations, advanced layouts, longer prompts, and custom themes.

In addition, your [custom branding](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding)
, [custom instructions](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/custom-instructions)
, and [presets](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets)
 are shared across your team, to help you maintain consistency across your slides and presentations.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-for-teams#invite-and-manage-your-team)

Invite and manage your team


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To invite your team, launch the Plus AI add-on in [Google Slides](https://slides.new/)
 (or add-in in PowerPoint).

Then click on "**Manage your team**" to add or remove teammates. When you invite a teammate, they will receive an email with a link to join the team.

You can also rename your organization and upload a logo.

If you're on a paid plan, you will automatically be billed for adding additional team members. [Learn more about plans and billing.](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FETmzOwqzVOWsoUNBJwr2%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.29.40%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfb2d431f-d868-4af4-8b6a-b0a8942f8c1d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1616d362&sv=2)

Managing your team in the Plus add-on

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-for-teams#joining-a-team)

Joining a team


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you're invited to a team in Plus, you should receive an email with a direct link to join.

If you can't find the email, you can also see **open invitations** in the accounts menu in the add-on in (Google Slides or PowerPoint) and the account portal: [https://app.plusdocs.com/ai-home](https://app.plusdocs.com/ai-home)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FDjHFrHGjDl5YJV6MQuWo%252FCleanShot%25202025-06-30%2520at%252010.19.26%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d3726c8-c0d3-43e5-b5c0-868fcf75d6e2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ce0e817f&sv=2)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-for-teams#what-if-im-a-part-of-multiple-teams)

What if I'm a part of multiple teams?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you're a member of multiple teams, you can switch between them in the Plus AI extension. Click on the square button next to the Plus logo. Then select the organization you want to use.

This can be useful if you (or your teammate) signed up for Plus as an individual before being invited to your team.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FIn9mXYPjKgBRJ9hMgdSe%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.34.25%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D84ca9bcc-d1a7-4ae3-b9e4-eaaba75a4486&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5f34ce2d&sv=2)

Switching organizations in the Plus add-on

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-for-teams#organization-owners)

Organization owners


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The user who created the organization is the organization owner. **Only the org owner can upgrade to a paid plan**, change plans, cancel an existing subscription.

👉 If you need to change the owner of your team, [contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-for-teams#team-permission-details)

Team permission details


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-for-teams#paid-plan-features)

Paid plan features

*   All paid plan features are available to everyone on a team.
    
*   Your organization owner will automatically be billed for every member of the team. [Learn more about plans and billing here.](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing)
    

**Plan and billing**

*   Only the organization owner can upgrade, downgrade, or cancel the team's paid plan (subscription). The organization owner is also the billing admin and receives subscription invoices.
    
*   If you need to change the owner of your team, [contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
    .
    
*   Any team member can invite new team members.
    

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-for-teams#custom-branding)

Custom branding

[Custom branding](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding)
 is shared across your team.

*   Every team member can edit your custom brand settings.
    
*   Every team member can use your custom branding when generating new presentations and editing slides.
    

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-for-teams#custom-instructions)

Custom instructions

Custom instructions are shared across your team. [Learn more about custom instructions.](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/custom-instructions)

*   There is a single set of custom instructions that are shared across your team.
    
*   Any team member can edit it.
    
*   All team members can choose whether to use your custom instructions when generating new presentations and slides.
    

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-for-teams#more-questions)

More questions?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)

# How to write a good prompt | Plus Guide

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/how-to-write-a-good-prompt#structuring-your-prompt)

Structuring your prompt


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here are some quick tips. You can read more on our [blog](https://www.plusdocs.com/blog/how-to-write-an-effective-ai-prompt)
.

*   Include context about the type of presentation and audience.
    
*   In addition to the overall topic, you can also ask for specific content to be included.
    

Remember you can always use text to presentation and slide-by-slide mode if you need more control than a short prompt.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FxLP6codXCMTeRTeWk0k4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De401db76-6970-4fac-afad-e00b8a1377e0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=894992ba&sv=2)

Save this cheatsheet for writing a good AI prompt.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/how-to-write-a-good-prompt#dos-and-donts)

Do's and Don'ts


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here are some types of instructions that don't work well with Plus AI and suggestions for what to do instead.

*   ❌ **Don’t** put specific design instructions in the prompt. Plus AI will ignore your instructions about colors and fonts. ✅ **Do:** Create a [custom theme](https://guide.plusdocs.com/plus-ai/custom-themes)
     to use when generating presentations.
    
*   ❌ **Don’t** add instructions about the number of slides in your prompt. ✅ **Do:** Use the dropdown in the add-on to select the exact number of slides you want. (If these instructions conflict, Plus AI tends to get quite confused 🥴)
    
*   ❌ **Don’t** ask Plus AI to create a presentation on current events. Plus AI doesn’t know about them. ✅ **Do:** Use [text to presentation](https://guide.plusdocs.com/plus-ai/generate-a-presentation/text-to-presentation)
     mode to paste in a news article or other document and transform it into a presentation.
    
*   ❌ **Don't** add URLs in the prompt for Plus AI. It will not be able to navigate to them to read or digest your website or document. ✅ **Do:** Use [text to presentation](https://guide.plusdocs.com/plus-ai/generate-a-presentation/text-to-presentation)
     mode to paste in the content that you want Plus to summarize.
    

[PreviousSlide by slide](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/slide-by-slide)
[NextInsert a single slide](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide)

# Presets | Plus Guide

Your team library includes **Custom instructions** and **Presets** to help you (and your team) save time when making new presentations.

You can access the team library from the New Presentation add-on. (In Google Slides, go to Extensions > Plus AI > New Presentation).

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets#custom-instructions)

Custom instructions

Instead of always having to add the same snippets to give Plus AI context when generating new presentations, you can save that information here once.

Your team has a single set of custom instructions.

Learn more:

[Custom instructions](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/custom-instructions)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets#presets)

Presets

If you tend to make the same type of presentation over and over, you can save these prompts and settings as presets.

For example, you can create a preset for a client proposal deck and another for a customer business review.

Learn more:

[Prompt presets](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/prompt-presets)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F4L5WtZHhuEtHpdruTGZ3%252FCleanShot%25202023-10-25%2520at%252014.59.01%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D544e8048-56c0-4982-8e02-b0fe6bb9c295&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d2935103&sv=2)

# Plus AI plans and billing | Plus Guide

For our latest plans and pricing, refer to our marketing website: [https://www.plusdocs.com/pricing](https://www.plusdocs.com/pricing)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#free-trial)

Free trial

You need a paid plan to use Plus AI, but if you're new to Plus, all paid plans come with a 7 day free trial.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#paid-plans)

Paid plans

Select a Plus subscription based on what you need:

*   The **Basic** plan unlocks unlimited AI generation and editing in Google Slides and PowerPoint.
    
*   The **Pro** plan unlocks more features, like longer character limits on your prompts and the ability to [upload a document](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file)
     and convert it to a presentation.
    
*   The **Team** plan allows you to save custom brand colors, fonts, and upload a logo to use when generating presentations. It also unlocks collaboration features like saved presets and custom instructions.
    

Paid plans are priced per user. If your organization has multiple users, the entire org will be upgraded, and we will automatically calculate the price at checkout. You cannot upgrade individual users in an organization.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#how-do-free-trials-work)

How do free trials work


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You need a paid plan to generate presentations in Google Slides or PowerPoint.

Starting a free trial requires a credit card, which will be automatically charged at the end of the 7 day trial period. You can [cancel](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#cancel-my-subscription)
 at any time during your trial to avoid getting charged.

Free trials are limited to new Plus customers, so if you've previously signed up for our free plan (no longer supported) or upgraded to one of our paid plans, unfortunately you do not qualify for the free trial.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#how-to-upgrade-to-a-paid-plan)

How to upgrade to a paid plan


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Only the owner of an organization can upgrade

Open the Plus AI add-on in Google Slides or the add-in in PowerPoint.

Click on **Upgrade** or **Manage Plans and Billing** under settings.

Select a plan and you'll be taken to Stripe (our payment processor) to complete checkout.

Our paid plans are subscriptions that will automatically renew every month or every year unless you [cancel](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#cancel-my-subscription)
. We do not issue refunds for subscription payments, so make sure you remember to cancel.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#using-a-coupon-code)

Using a coupon code

If you have a coupon or discount code, you can apply it at checkout.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#manage-or-cancel-my-subscription)

Manage or cancel my subscription


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Only the owner of the organization can manage a paid plan.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#cancel-my-subscription)

Cancel my subscription

Cancel your paid plan at anytime from the Plus add-on. Open the Plus add-on and click **Plans and Billing.** Then click on the **Manage plan** button.

Alternatively, you can also access the Stripe billing portal directly: [https://app.plusdocs.com/billing-portal](https://app.plusdocs.com/billing-portal)

You will likely need to login again. Make sure you use the email address associated with your Plus account.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FsZmMLf7V0qHqzCzzggfk%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.26.33%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14fe5f15-f104-4e11-aafa-6c8d0639de32&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17a3bff3&sv=2)

Click on "Plans and Billing" to manage your Plus subscription within Google Slides or PowerPoint

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#upgrade-to-pro-or-team-plan)

Upgrade to Pro or Team plan

You can also upgrade to a Pro or Team plan from the same [billing portal](https://app.plusdocs.com/billing-portal)
.

When you upgrade to a higher tiered plan, you'll be billed immediately for the difference between the two plans, pro-rated for the amount of time left in the billing cycle.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#change-to-a-different-billing-frequency)

Change to a different billing frequency

You can also change from monthly billing to annual billing (or vice versa) in the same billing portal.

The same pro-ration logic applies. If you're switching from an annual plan to a monthly plan, your account will be credited for the payment you already made for your annual plan, which will be applied to your future monthly payments.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#faqs)

FAQs


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Which plan is right for me?[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#which-plan-is-right-for-me)

If you just want to unlock unlimited AI, get the **Basic** plan.

If you need more advanced features, especially custom themes or longer prompts for your slides, get the **Pro** plan.

How do Plus subscriptions work?[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#how-do-plus-subscriptions-work)

Prices are based on the number of users in your team. Paid plans are billed either monthly or annually, depending on what you choose.

You can [cancel](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#cancel-my-subscription)
 your paid subscription at any time, but we do not offer refunds on subscription payments.

Do I need separate subscriptions for Google Slides and PowerPoint?[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#do-i-need-separate-subscriptions-for-google-slides-and-powerpoint)

Your Plus AI subscription includes both Google Slides and PowerPoint. You can use Plus AI in both apps if you want.

How does the free trial work?[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#how-does-the-free-trial-work)

New Plus customers can try a paid plan for 7 days before committing. Free trials require a credit card, but you can cancel at any time during the trial period.

[See above for more details.](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#how-do-free-trials-work)

How do I cancel my subscription?[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#how-do-i-cancel-my-subscription)

Go to the billing portal: [https://app.plusdocs.com/billing-portal](https://app.plusdocs.com/billing-portal)

You will likely need to login again. Make sure you login with the email address associated with your Plus account.

Does uninstalling the Google Workspace add-on (or the PowerPoint add-in) cancel my Plus subscription?[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#does-uninstalling-the-google-workspace-add-on-or-the-powerpoint-add-in-cancel-my-plus-subscription)

No! Uninstalling the Google add-on or Microsoft add-in does not cancel your Plus subscription or delete your Plus account.

Please make sure you [cancel](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#cancel-my-subscription)
 your subscription to avoid getting charged.

Can I have a refund?[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#can-i-have-a-refund)

We don't offer refunds on paid subscriptions. Make sure you remember to [cancel](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#cancel-my-subscription)
 your subscription if you don't want to be charged.

If you ran into a specific problem while using Plus, please [let us know](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

Refer to our [terms of service](https://www.plusdocs.com/terms)
 for details.

Why should I invite someone to my team?[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#why-should-i-invite-someone-to-my-team)

Team members have access to paid plan features, including longer character limits for prompts and a shared library of themes.

You will be billed for each additional team member you invite.

What happens when I upgrade or downgrade?[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#what-happens-when-i-upgrade-or-downgrade)

When you upgrade to a more expensive plan, Stripe (our payment provider) will automatically calculate the difference between the new plan and the current plan, prorated for the amount of time remaining in your billing cycle (either monthly or annually).

You'll be immediately billed for that pro-rated difference, then continue to be billed for the new plan amount on your regular billing date.

When you downgrade, Stripe will calculate the same pro-rated difference, which will be applied to your account as a credit. That credit will be automatically applied to future payments. Note that your account is not credited if you cancel your paid plan completely.

What happens when I invite (or remove) team members?[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#what-happens-when-i-invite-or-remove-team-members)

On monthly plans, you'll see a prorated charge for the new team member on your next month's bill, in addition to the regular price for that team member.

Example: Chloe upgrades to the Slides plan as a single user, then invites Dan after a couple of weeks. Her monthly bills look like this:

*   Month 1: $10 ($10 x 1 user)
    
*   Month 2: $25 ($10 x 2 users + 50 x $10 x 1 user (Dan for half of the previous month)
    

On annual plans, you'll immediately be billed for the prorated cost of the new member.

If you remove a team member, your account will be credited for the prorated remainder of that user's subscription, which will automatically be applied to your next bill.

I need an invoice or receipt for my subscription[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#i-need-an-invoice-or-receipt-for-my-subscription)

Go to the Stripe billing portal: [https://app.plusdocs.com/billing-portal](https://app.plusdocs.com/billing-portal)

You will likely need to login again. Make sure you login with the email address associated with your Plus account. You should then be redirected to Stripe (our payment provider). If not, go that URL again after logging in.

You'll be able to view previous payments and download those invoices.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#more-questions-get-in-touch)

More questions? Get in touch


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)

[PreviousPowerPoint desktop app recommended](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint/powerpoint-desktop-app-recommended)
[NextPlus AI for teams](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-for-teams)

Last updated 9 months ago

# Languages | Plus Guide

Plus AI supports prompts and outputs in most languages. You can specify the language you want Plus to generate content in.

You can also use [rewrite](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/rewrite-slides)
 to translate existing slides and presentations into another language.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/languages#generating-slides-in-a-specific-language)

Generating slides in a specific language


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When [generating a new presentation](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation)
 or [inserting a single slide](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide)
, you can specify what language you want Plus to write in. It does not have to match your input language, Plus will understand most languages.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F9pcqerpSyqG6zYO0Ymlo%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.22.27%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D614bc613-ceb2-4761-ba9c-ca9f208746ca&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=123c94b5&sv=2)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/languages#translate-slides-into-another-language)

Translate slides into another language


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use [rewrite](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/rewrite-slides)
 to translate an existing slide into a different language. You can rewrite a single slide or your entire presentation at once.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F5eixSOLQdNFYU2B2Bhyr%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-14%2520at%252010.43.38%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c7f8c30-b349-4632-8599-283902c8d795&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=abdca99a&sv=2)

Translating a slide from English to Spanish with Plus AI

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/languages#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Like other generative AI tools, Plus AI can occasionally behave inconsistently. If you get a slide in the wrong language, we recommend just trying it again.

If you consistently have issues with languages or have other questions, [let us know](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

[PreviousRemix slides](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/remix-slides)
[NextTemplates](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/templates)

# Generate a presentation | Plus Guide

Use Plus AI to create a Google Slides presentation from scratch, in just a few minutes. You can start with a short prompt, a long document or article, or build your presentation slide-by-slide.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation#generate-a-presentation)

Generate a presentation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation#google-slides)

Google Slides

To create a new presentation, [create a new Google Slides](https://slides.new/)
 presentation, then launch the Plus add-on from the Extensions menu: **Extensions** > **Plus AI for Google Slides** > **New Presentation**.

![A screenshot of launching the Plus AI add-on in Google Slides by going to Extensions, Plus AI for Google Slides, and then New presentation.](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FoUDTqKIO1yFfzlg797G6%252FCleanShot%25202023-09-21%2520at%252010.36.32%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3eb4ad8e-4e24-457c-ae88-4320159f567c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aea6d940&sv=2)

Open the Plus add-on from Google Slides by going to Extensions > Plus AI for Google Slides

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation#powerpoint)

PowerPoint

Go to the **Home** tab, click on **Add-ins.** Search for Plus AI if it doesn't show up immediately under My Add-ins

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F5I8hq5Odi9SmhlwkeeFG%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-13%2520at%252014.48.13%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44b1143f-3ff6-4997-b1fc-79be41aec12d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7cd26334&sv=2)

Launch Plus AI in PowerPoint: Go to Home > Add-ins. Search for Plus AI if it doesn't show up.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation#presentation-modes)

Presentation modes


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are three ways to generate a new presentation. (Click through to learn more about each.) If you start from a template, you can still use any mode you like.

1.  [**Use a prompt**](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/use-a-prompt)
     You provide a short prompt, like "Create a presentation explaining quantum entanglement to 5th graders." This is the easiest way to get started.
    
2.  [**Upload a file**](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file)
     **(⭐ Most popular option)** You can upload a PDF, Word Document, text file (or paste in unformatted text) and convert it into well-formatted slides.
    
3.  [**Slide by slide**](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/slide-by-slide)
     You can build your presentation one slide at a time and specify the content on each slide. This is the most time consuming, but offers the most control.
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fh4jKIsI9frSpaiVzDvTt%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.20.00%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e5d5a08-0148-499b-86b2-535b7e325a00&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c30746cb&sv=2)

Start a new presentation in the Plus add-on

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation#edit-with-plus-ai)

Edit with Plus AI

After generating your presentation (or if you have an existing presentation), use our editing tools to continue to refine your presentation.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/rewrite-slides)

![Cover](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FetbuS1hqd4pQEy72HSAC%252Frewrite.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De01ceecf-ed7e-46a3-9670-fc24dd20429f&width=245&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8fcfeca1&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation#rewrite-content)

Change the tone or audience

# Insert a single slide | Plus Guide

You can use Plus to generate a single slide in a specific format. This gives you a lot more control over the layout of the individual slide, vs letting AI pick for you when generating an entire presentation.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide#launch-edit-with-plus-ai)

Launch Edit with Plus AI


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Google Slides[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide#google-slides)

Launch Google Slides (Here is a shortcut: [https://slides.new](https://slides.new/)
).

In Google Slides, go to **Extensions** > **Plus AI for Google Slides** > **Edit with Plus AI**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fko9MlfUsetIYXIUPxFgu%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-14%2520at%252010.02.15%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5e02c22-8a3f-4df7-9b1e-62a786fecf9f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=85277175&sv=2)

**Troubleshooting:**

*   If you don't see Plus AI in the Extensions menu, make sure you have it [installed](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides)
    .
    
*   If you don't see any options under Plus AI (except "Help"), reload the page in your browser and give it a minute to load.
    
*   Check out our [troubleshooting guide](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting)
    .
    

PowerPoint[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide#powerpoint)

In PowerPoint, go to the **Home** tab of the menu > **Add-ins** \> **Plus AI**. (Search for Plus AI if it does not appear)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F5I8hq5Odi9SmhlwkeeFG%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-13%2520at%252014.48.13%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44b1143f-3ff6-4997-b1fc-79be41aec12d&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7cd26334&sv=2)

In the Plus AI sidebar, click on **Edit with AI** and select **Insert a Slide**.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide#add-a-single-slide)

Add a single slide


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Make sure you're on the **Insert** tab of the Edit with Plus AI menu.

Enter a slide **title**, **description**, and select the **slide layout** you want. Click **Generate slide.**

The new slide will be inserted into your presentation, which you can edit freely, just like any other Google Slide or PowerPoint slide.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FMHwxUFGZ7sETwAX3ppG9%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-14%2520at%252010.28.02%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc067b0f-7a81-420a-900b-b2fa67b82f44&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e42132&sv=2)

Inserting a single slide using Plus AI for Google Slides

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FyDIc8RXgNv0PrzU9RDbY%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-25%2520at%252016.23.23%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0350719e-4779-437d-af9e-23292be1b7e5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cb3eef3a&sv=2)

# Slide by slide | Plus Guide

**Slide by slide** mode lets you build a presentation one slide at a time. Instead of writing one prompt for the entire presentation, you can specify exactly what you want on each slide. If you'd like, you can also choose a specific layout for each slide.

**Slide by slide** mode is useful if you have a very specific _content structure_ in mind and want more control than [starting from a prompt](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/use-a-prompt)
 will allow, but you're not working off an [existing document or article](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file)
.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/slide-by-slide#how-to-use-slide-by-slide-mode)

How to use Slide by slide mode


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Launch Plus AI in [Google Slides](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides)
 or [PowerPoint](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint)
.

Click on **Slide by slide.**

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/slide-by-slide#set-up-your-presentation)

Set up your presentation

In the left panel, you can add a presentation title and additional instructions on voice and tone.

You can also add and delete slides to change the length of your presentation.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/slide-by-slide#add-content-to-each-slide)

Add content to each slide

Click on each slide to edit it.

Add a slide title and slide content. You can add as much or as little detail as you'd like (up to 5,000 characters per slide.)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/slide-by-slide#select-a-layout)

Select a layout

If you'd like, you can choose a specific layout for each slide. Or you can just leave it on auto and have Plus AI choose.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FyiLrNgbIn7ZYG8aWsnb6%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252016.10.01%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd668758d-a16a-4f5c-928f-043127eaab12&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6bc64048&sv=2)

Slide by slide mode in Plus

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/slide-by-slide#generate-slides)

Generate slides

When you're happy with your outline, Plus AI will proceed by generating the slides in your presentation.

If you did not start from a template, you can choose a presentation **theme**. Themes allow you to choose the visual look and feel of your slides, including fonts and colors. Pro users can create and save [custom themes](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding)
.

Newly generated slides are added to the end of your presentation. If you didn't start with a blank file, scroll down to find your new slides.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FUc2ROeNoqlN8edSTkCdf%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.54.01%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D532a1efe-3680-499a-a325-618f51f01bd9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f735cb2c&sv=2)

When your presentation is generated, the Plus AI generate window will close. You can keep editing with Plus.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/slide-by-slide#editing-your-presentation)

Editing your presentation

After your presentation is created, the add-on will close automatically.

At this point, your slides work just like any other Google Slides (or PowerPoint slides). You can edit them directly, share them, or export them as a PDF or other file type.

The Edit with Plus AI sidebar will open automatically to help you continue to refine your deck.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/slide-by-slide#learn-more-about-editing-with-plus-ai)

Learn more about editing with Plus AI

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/rewrite-slides)

![Cover](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FetbuS1hqd4pQEy72HSAC%252Frewrite.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De01ceecf-ed7e-46a3-9670-fc24dd20429f&width=245&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8fcfeca1&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/slide-by-slide#rewrite-content)

Rewrite content

Change the tone or audience

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide)

# History | Plus Guide

You can find and reuse the previous presentations you've generated in the history view.

Only you can see your prompt history. It is not shared with your team.

This is a new feature we added on October 15, 2023, so the presentations you generated since then will appear in your History.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/history#view-your-history)

View your history


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Launch Plus AI in [Google Slides](https://slides.new/)
. (Extensions > Plus AI for Google Slides > New Presentation.)

![A screenshot of launching the Plus AI add-on in Google Slides by going to Extensions, Plus AI for Google Slides, and then New presentation.](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FoUDTqKIO1yFfzlg797G6%252FCleanShot%25202023-09-21%2520at%252010.36.32%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3eb4ad8e-4e24-457c-ae88-4320159f567c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aea6d940&sv=2)

Open the Plus add-on from Google Slides by going to Extensions > Plus AI for Google Slides

Click on **History** in the left-hand navigation panel.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FuaoGFUcCIYSuNG4S4qU5%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252016.17.27%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e458bc4-a5ee-4193-b2c9-6f6c48b7d6b2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2264a0f9&sv=2)

The history tab in Plus

From here you can see:

*   The date when you generated the presentation
    
*   The mode you used (i.e., [start from a prompt](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/use-a-prompt)
    , [text to presentation](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file)
    , or [slide by slide](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/slide-by-slide)
    )
    
*   A preview of the prompt you used
    

For every presentation in your history, you can:

*   **Open.** This opens the link to the Google Slides file where you used Plus AI to generate this presentation in a new tab. Note that if you edited or deleted the slides after generating them, you cannot restore them. This simply opens that file.
    
*   **Reuse.** This launches the presentation generator with the same prompt(s) and settings filled in, which you can then edit, just like when generating a brand new presentation. You can also click reuse to see what you prompt you used without proceeding to the "generate" step.
    

[PreviousCustom branding](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding)
[NextPresets](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Prompt presets | Plus Guide

Presets require the [Pro plan](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing)
.

Presets allow you and your team to save frequently used prompts and settings to your team library, to save you time when generating new presentations.

Unlike [custom instructions](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/custom-instructions)
, which is a single set of instructions shared across presentations, you can save different presets for different types of documents, like one for a client proposal deck and another for a customer business review.

Presets are shared across your team.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FaUvIPzEf4hvbrRbnHcbn%252F2023-11-06%2520preset.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D288ea051-70eb-462d-bfed-376f56878e8c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9ab2f7b2&sv=2)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/prompt-presets#accessing-your-preset-library)

Accessing your preset library


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Launch Plus AI in [Google Slides](https://slides.new/)
. (Extensions > Plus AI for Google Slides > New Presentation.)

![A screenshot of launching the Plus AI add-on in Google Slides by going to Extensions, Plus AI for Google Slides, and then New presentation.](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FoUDTqKIO1yFfzlg797G6%252FCleanShot%25202023-09-21%2520at%252010.36.32%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3eb4ad8e-4e24-457c-ae88-4320159f567c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aea6d940&sv=2)

Open the Plus add-on from Google Slides by going to Extensions > Plus AI for Google Slides

Click on **Team Library** in the left-hand navigation panel. Then click on **Presets.**

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F18eNp5aDdLuOOPl29A2q%252FCleanShot%25202023-10-25%2520at%252015.05.45%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc826c1a8-12ce-43a4-beca-ad2d6b33255b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9e4f420a&sv=2)

Presets are shared across your team. Anyone can create, edit, and use them.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/prompt-presets#creating-a-preset)

Creating a preset


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can create a preset directly from the preset library or from your [History](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/history)
.

**From your preset library**, click **Create new preset**, select a mode, and then add your prompts, instructions, and settings. Give your preset a name and click save.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FlJTL9nuvsRuhUpr0fOcN%252FCleanShot%25202023-10-25%2520at%252015.07.04%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77b34802-d3af-42ef-948e-b6ce3be14514&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=597f8b1c&sv=2)

How to create a preset in Plus AI from scratch

**From your prompt history,** click the **Save** button next to one of your previously generated presentations to create a preset. You can edit your prompts, instructions, and settings. Then give your preset a name and click save.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FCYYXAJAKy3rcPVPWpraW%252FCleanShot%25202023-10-25%2520at%252015.13.48%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b07027f-4d0b-4431-b400-b6a647819970&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81705c6f&sv=2)

Create a preset from a presentation in your history by clicking "Save"

You can come back to the preset library to edit the preset at any time.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/prompt-presets#using-presets)

Using presets


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To create a new presentation from a preset, Go to your **Team Library** > **Presets** and click **Use** in the Preset library or select a preset during the presentation process.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F7jm6E4EY1qqY2BW5SIxv%252FCleanShot%25202023-10-25%2520at%252015.20.11%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c05e307-c366-4baf-9747-71ddec261abc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1c6209c8&sv=2)

When you select a preset, your saved prompts, instructions, and settings will be applied. You can then make any tweaks or adjustments you'd like before proceeding with generating a presentation, just as you would if you were starting from scratch.

Edits you make after applying a preset will not automatically be saved to that preset. For example, you may want to use placeholders in your preset (e.g., "\[client name here\]") that you edit when generating the actual presentation.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/prompt-presets#editing-and-deleting-presets)

Editing and deleting presets


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Anyone on the team can update and delete presets from the preset library.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/prompt-presets#how-do-presets-work-with-custom-instructions)

How do presets work with custom instructions?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Both presets and [custom instructions](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/custom-instructions)
 allow you (and your team) to save content for reuse with Plus AI. There's no hard or fast rule for when to use each.

We recommend using **custom instructions** **for context that Plus AI should always keep in mind**, like information about your company or a preferred writing style. Every team has exactly one set of custom instructions.

We recommend using **presets** **to save specific types of presentations that you make frequently**, like one for a client proposal, another for a business review. You can create as many presets as you would like.

You do not need to repeat the information saved in your custom instructions in your presets. When you configure a preset, you can specify whether your custom instructions should be included or not.

[PreviousCustom instructions](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/custom-instructions)
[NextGenerate images with AI](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-images-with-ai)

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

# Rewrite slides | Plus Guide

Use **Rewrite** to improve phrasing, change your tone, lengthen or shorten something, and translate your presentation.

If you want to change the layout or design of your slide, use [**Remix**](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/remix-slides)
 instead.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/rewrite-slides#launch-edit-with-plus-ai)

Launch Edit with Plus AI


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Google Slides[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/rewrite-slides#google-slides)

Launch Google Slides (Here is a shortcut: [https://slides.new](https://slides.new/)
).

In Google Slides, go to **Extensions** > **Plus AI for Google Slides** > **Edit with Plus AI**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fko9MlfUsetIYXIUPxFgu%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-14%2520at%252010.02.15%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5e02c22-8a3f-4df7-9b1e-62a786fecf9f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=85277175&sv=2)

**Troubleshooting:**

*   If you don't see Plus AI in the Extensions menu, make sure you have it [installed](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides)
    .
    
*   If you don't see any options under Plus AI (except "Help"), reload the page in your browser and give it a minute to load.
    
*   Check out our [troubleshooting guide](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting)
    .
    

PowerPoint[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/rewrite-slides#powerpoint)

In PowerPoint, go to the **Home** tab of the menu > **Add-ins** \> **Plus AI**. (Search for Plus AI if it does not appear)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F5I8hq5Odi9SmhlwkeeFG%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-13%2520at%252014.48.13%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44b1143f-3ff6-4997-b1fc-79be41aec12d&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7cd26334&sv=2)

In the Plus AI sidebar, click on **Edit with AI** and select **Rewrite**.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/rewrite-slides#rewrite-a-slide)

Rewrite a slide


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Select the **Rewrite** tab, add a prompt or select a (customizable) preset.

You can rewrite a specific text element, a single slide, or your entire presentation.

**Pro-tip:** You can undo + redo these changes in Google Slides. Duplicate your slide before using Rewrite if you want to produce multiple options that you can review.

You can rewrite your slide as many times as you want. Sometimes it's helpful to string together multiple rewrites, for example, embellishing some copy for a product page, then asking Plus AI to help you make it more succinct.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FPVhcPzaZkkBcQcw4GAg7%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-14%2520at%252011.02.28%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6d47f20f-6109-4168-9eda-9588da581886&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a089731&sv=2)

Rewriting a slide in Plus AI

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FZTIhnxRXBueKDIwZOYLz%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-25%2520at%252016.25.31%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D01e2b159-cfae-4c13-91dd-dc0079968990&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=32071c58&sv=2)

Using rewrite to translate a slide in Plus AI for PowerPoint

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/rewrite-slides#translate-slides)

Translate slides


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can also use rewrite to translate your presentation.

Select the **Language** you want to translate _**to**_. (For example, if your slide is in English and you want to translate it into Spanish, select Español in the dropdown.)

Click on the **Translate** preset, which will populate the rewrite instructions.

You can rewrite a single slide or your entire presentation (this can take a few minutes.)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F5eixSOLQdNFYU2B2Bhyr%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-14%2520at%252010.43.38%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c7f8c30-b349-4632-8599-283902c8d795&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=abdca99a&sv=2)

Using Plus AI to translate a slide from English to Spanish.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/rewrite-slides#do-more-with-plus-ai)

Do more with Plus AI

# Remix slides | Plus Guide

**Remix** is a useful tool for reformatting a slide — whether that's an existing slide design or just a blob of text you've pasted onto your slide. Plus AI can transform the content to fit the layout you want.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fh00OR0QIcCTeMW0t7fJA%252F2025%252007%252001%2520remix.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ef67fd5-ec40-4d04-b468-40f250e1a364&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=501441b6&sv=2)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/remix-slides#launch-edit-with-plus-ai)

Launch Edit with Plus AI


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Google Slides[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/remix-slides#google-slides)

Launch Google Slides (Here is a shortcut: [https://slides.new](https://slides.new/)
).

In Google Slides, go to **Extensions** > **Plus AI for Google Slides** > **Edit with Plus AI**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fko9MlfUsetIYXIUPxFgu%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-14%2520at%252010.02.15%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5e02c22-8a3f-4df7-9b1e-62a786fecf9f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=85277175&sv=2)

In the Plus AI sidebar, click on **Edit with AI** and select **Insert a Slide**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FdrFrk5GJQIwB4QlIfyua%252FCleanShot%25202025-07-01%2520at%252011.10.47%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfcc0914f-1815-4ee4-b0f7-d13e0d5905e4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9e060ff1&sv=2)

PowerPoint[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/remix-slides#powerpoint)

In PowerPoint, go to the **Home** tab of the menu > **Add-ins** \> **Plus AI**. (Search for Plus AI if it does not appear)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F5I8hq5Odi9SmhlwkeeFG%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-13%2520at%252014.48.13%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44b1143f-3ff6-4997-b1fc-79be41aec12d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7cd26334&sv=2)

In the Plus AI sidebar, click on **Edit with AI** and select **Insert a Slide**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FSkM0q6XjIGzg0gpniH4a%252FCleanShot%25202025-07-01%2520at%252011.10.47%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df8d3b509-bfd2-4ae4-81fc-a3e4e2590412&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6bf6f989&sv=2)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/remix-slides#remix-a-slide)

Remix a slide


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Make sure you're on the **Remix** tab of the Edit with Plus sidebar.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FyVanvinAKtgl6uEJQF8q%252FCleanShot%25202025-07-01%2520at%252011.13.43%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99eaa9b8-6ba8-4948-93fc-593a47ad01a3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=85356a22&sv=2)

*   Make sure the slide you want to remix is selected in Google Slides or PowerPoint
    
*   Choose the mode you want
    
    *   **Default:** Your text will be rewritten — shorted or expanded — as needed to fit the slide layout
        
    *   **Strict:** Your text will be preserved as much as possible, which means it might not fill up or fit the output slide well.
        
    
*   In Plus AI, select the template you want to use. If you've generated a Plus AI presentation in the same file, the template you used will be automatically selected.
    
*   Select a layout — this is the what your slide will be reformatted _into_
    
*   Click **Remix** **Current Slide**
    

**Pro-tip:** You can undo + redo these changes. Duplicate your slide before using Remix if you want to produce multiple options that you can review.

Last updated 25 days ago

Was this helpful?
