# Custom instructions | Plus Guide

Use custom instructions to save important context about you or your team that Plus AI should remember every time it generates a presentation. Custom instructions saves time because you don't have to provide the same prompts over and over to Plus AI.

Custom instructions are shared across your team.

Custom instructions requires a paid **Pro** plan. [Learn more about our plans.](https://www.plusdocs.com/pricing)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FVwZk63Sl8ZcX6mgbGXQ5%252FCleanShot%25202023-10-25%2520at%252015.04.17%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfbb83e5c-0c43-487b-9b13-9b45dcdc0d6d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b0edd0ed&sv=2)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/custom-instructions#set-custom-instructions)

Set custom instructions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Launch Plus AI in [Google Slides](https://slides.new/)
. (Extensions > Plus AI for Google Slides > New Presentation.)

![A screenshot of launching the Plus AI add-on in Google Slides by going to Extensions, Plus AI for Google Slides, and then New presentation.](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FoUDTqKIO1yFfzlg797G6%252FCleanShot%25202023-09-21%2520at%252010.36.32%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3eb4ad8e-4e24-457c-ae88-4320159f567c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aea6d940&sv=2)

Open the Plus add-on from Google Slides by going to Extensions > Plus AI for Google Slides

Click on **Team Library** in the menu, then **Custom instructions** (this is the default)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fh0AjLfMG8zv5cLZ9d0Dj%252FCleanShot%25202023-10-25%2520at%252015.05.04%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5e0a3fd-778a-4cd7-99bc-8e20468bf484&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6fc6b20f&sv=2)

Enter your custom instructions, then click **Save**. You can come back to this page to edit your custom instructions at any time.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/custom-instructions#custom-instructions-are-shared-with-your-team)

Custom instructions are shared with your team

Keep this in mind when you write custom instructions if you're on a team using Plus.

Using custom instructions can help your team get consistent outputs from Plus AI. For example, you can maintain one set of prompts that describes your company.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/custom-instructions#using-custom-instructions)

Using custom instructions


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, custom instructions are included every time you generate a new presentation.

You can also choose to turn off custom instructions when generating a presentation. This can be useful if, for example, your custom instructions are related to your work, but you want to generate a fun presentation for personal use.

[PreviousPresets](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets)
[NextPrompt presets](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/prompt-presets)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Copyright | Plus Guide

Plus respects the intellectual property rights of others and expect our users to do the same. In accordance with the [Digital Millennium Copyright Act of 1998](https://www.copyright.gov/legislation/dmca.pdf)
 (DMCA), Plus will respond expeditiously to claims of copyright infringement committed using Plus.

If you are a copyright owner, authorized to act on behalf of one, or authorized to act under any exclusive right under copyright, please [contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
 to report alleged copyright infringements taking place on or through Plus.

We reserve the right to delete or disable content alleged to be infringing and terminate accounts of repeat infringers.

# Contact us | Plus Guide

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us#get-in-touch)

Get in touch


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you need additional help, email us at [\[email protected\]](https://guide.plusai.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#364543464659444276465a4345525955451855595b)
.

We have a small team, so it can take up to a couple of business days for us to get back to you.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us#information-to-include)

Information to include

Please [double check your account email](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#im-signed-into-the-wrong-account)
 before contacting us. Make a note if it's different than the email you're writing from.

To help us assist you more quickly, please provide as much detail as possible in your initial outreach. Include the following detail, based on what you need.

Billing[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us#billing)

*   Attach or include a screenshot of your invoice
    
*   Review the FAQs here [Plus AI plans and billing](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing)
    

Using the add-on[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us#using-the-add-on)

*   Indicate whether you use Google Slides or PowerPoint (or both)
    
*   Describe your issue in as much detail as possible, including your inputs and outputs
    
    *   Include the prompt you used
        
    *   Attach a copy of any files you uploaded
        
    *   Include a link or attach a copy of your presentation, if possible
        
    
*   Include a screen recording or screenshots, if possible
    

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us#faqs)

# Generate a new document | Plus Guide

Use Plus AI to draft new blog posts, articles, lesson plans, and other text content in just a few seconds.

Using Plus AI in Google Docs to generate, restructure, and translate content.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-google-docs/generate-a-new-document#launch-plus-ai-in-google-docs)

Launch Plus AI in Google Docs


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a [new Google Doc](http://docs.new/)
 or open an existing one, then launch the Plus add-on from the Extensions menu: **Extensions** > **Plus AI** > **Edit with Plus AI**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F1pGHFopGTibj32QgU23I%252FCleanShot%25202024-02-06%2520at%252016.26.47%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0e08395c-4187-43ea-ba85-623a64b3ade0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3ef6433c&sv=2)

Open the Plus AI extension in Google Docs

You need a paid plan to use Plus AI. If you're a new customer to Plus, you can start a 7 day free trial. You'll need to add a credit card, but you can [cancel](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing#manage-or-cancel-my-subscription)
 at any time during your trial.

Learn more about our plans [here](https://www.plusdocs.com/pricing)
, and more about [billing](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing)
 here.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-google-docs/generate-a-new-document#generate-text)

Generate text


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the **Generate** tab, enter a prompt that describes what you want Plus AI to write, or use or start from one of our presets.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FTZDhqc9R2ZsLLHXJ5UIC%252FCleanShot%25202024-02-06%2520at%252016.32.00%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3c46653f-4f36-4f17-bf1c-9f7a40385b8e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61363d4d&sv=2)

Using a preset prompt in Plus AI for Google Docs

Click Generate and wait for Plus AI to write your content. This can take up to a minute or so for more complex prompts.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-google-docs/generate-a-new-document#languages)

Languages


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use the dropdown to select the language you want Plus AI to write in. Do not put this into your prompt directly.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-google-docs/generate-a-new-document#generate-more-content)

Generate more content


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use generate content as many times as you want. New text will be inserted at the end of your existing document.

You can also ask Plus AI to generate multiple variants of something in one go, which is especially useful for short-form content like ad copy or social media posts.

**Here's an example prompt:**

`Write three variants for a Facebook Ad for a subscription peanut butter company. Keep the headlines concise and make sure they appeal to busy moms.`

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-google-docs/generate-a-new-document#undo-and-redo)

Undo and redo


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use the native undo and redo actions in Google Docs on any Plus AI insertions or edits.

To undo, click the button in the Google Docs toolbar or press ⌘Z (or Ctrl + Z) on your keyboard.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FeydMMHPiTaeXMaNVwvyp%252FCleanShot%25202024-02-06%2520at%252016.36.46%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2952b87d-9aa8-4739-8bb4-327120de8537&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9aeb2801&sv=2)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-google-docs/generate-a-new-document#text-formatting)

Text formatting


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

While Plus AI can do basic formatting (paragraph breaks, headers, bullets and lists), it cannot do more advanced formatting, like changing colors or fonts, or add media like images or videos.

[PreviousGenerate images with AI](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-images-with-ai)
[NextEdit documents](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-google-docs/edit-documents)

# Chrome extension | Plus Guide

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/chrome-extension#installing-the-chrome-extension)

Installing the chrome extension


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You need the Chrome extension to take Snapshots. If you only plan to use Plus to view Snapshots other team members have taken, you do not need the extension.

Go to the [Plus extension in the Chrome store](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/plus/bnebanooamokkihfjepphafoekheipfh)
. Click the **Add to Chrome** button to install the extension. Then log into your Plus account.

We recommend "pinning" the extension so it is accessible for taking new Snapshots.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FjH3zEumUaufCMs70iIXS%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-24%2520at%252012.00.07.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7b12e78-bfbf-44ea-b5cb-3a96c124ef72&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=efa193a0&sv=2)

Pin the Plus extension for ease of access

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/chrome-extension#browser-support-for-the-extension)

Browser support for the extension

The extension is designed to be used with Google Chrome.

It will also work for other chromium-based browsers, including Microsoft Edge, Brave, and Arc.

The browser extension does not work on mobile devices, though you can view all the Snapshots you've captured on your phone in our web app.

[PreviousShare with others](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/share-with-others)
[NextUpdating the extension](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/chrome-extension/updating-the-extension)

Last updated 25 days ago

Was this helpful?

# Templates | Plus Guide

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/templates#what-are-templates)

What are templates?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Templates are existing presentation designs that Plus AI has been trained on. You can use templates when [generating a presentation](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation)
, [inserting](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide)
 a single slide, and [remixing](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/remix-slides)
 slides.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Flq82y5Z4IAb6MLomtdOg%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252016.16.43%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8fd42343-e824-476b-bd63-934d7cd23434&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6ea01790&sv=2)

Choosing a template when creating a presentation with Plus AI

Using a template is the easiest way to create a more visually distinct presentation than the default Plus AI designs, which are meant to be simple and minimal.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FMUIND4X2c9rUj47GRLr2%252Ftemplate%2520examples.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09f907a0-73ab-4511-a7b3-bcddbb20503d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c7706168&sv=2)

Comparing presentation generated using a template vs the default Plus AI designs.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/templates#using-templates)

Using templates


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use templates when [creating a new presentation](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation)
 and editing ([insert](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide)
 and [remix](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/remix-slides)
).

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/templates#new-presentation)

New presentation

Open the Plus add-on in Google Slides (Extensions > Plus AI for Google Slides > New Presentation).

Select **Use a template** mode. Choose your template. You can click on the thumbnail to see a preview of all the slide designs. Click **Use template** when you're ready to start.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FB2unSxRWm81RqFMxTuSg%252FCleanShot%25202024-03-19%2520at%252011.49.22%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De22413bb-45a0-4485-9a32-777ea9519307&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81c77412&sv=2)

Previewing a template in the Plus AI add-on

Once you've selected a template, you can still toggle between [Start from scratch](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/use-a-prompt)
, [Text to presentation](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file)
, and [Slide by slide](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/slide-by-slide)
 modes. Templates will work with all three.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FrgXCSSd21sUvpB65yAf4%252FCleanShot%25202024-03-19%2520at%252011.50.05%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9bdee841-9187-423a-b56d-6720b4961d3d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d16ebcf&sv=2)

You can toggle between all the modes of generating a presentation after you've selected a template.

Enter your prompt, paste your text, or upload your files as you would normally do. [Learn more about generating a presentation.](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/templates#editing-an-existing-presentation-with-templates)

Editing an existing presentation with templates

Templates also work with [Insert](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide)
 and [Remix](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/remix-slides)
. Select the template you want to use and you can see previews of each slide design available.

⚠️ Templates are not compatible with [custom themes](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding)
. If we detect that your presentation was generated using a template, the "Design" tab will not be available in the Edit sidebar.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FtQIYdGEedhVf5rGoNhBG%252FCleanShot%25202024-03-19%2520at%252011.53.34%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d82471f-a6ff-4f0f-aa99-511eda1adbe6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ab7515ce&sv=2)

You can use templates with Insert and Remix

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/templates#faq)

FAQ


------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/templates#how-are-templates-different-than-custom-branding)

How are templates different than custom branding?

Templates are not currently compatible with [custom branding](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding)
.

Reach out to us if you want to customize an existing template with your brand colors, fonts, and logo. We offer a "semi-custom" solution that is more affordable for small teams than our Enterprise solution.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/templates#how-do-i-upload-a-custom-template)

How do I upload a custom template?

Custom template upload is currently in beta in Google Slides.

Custom template upload only works well for templates that primarily contain text and images. Templates with lots of special slide types — charts, icons, diagrams — can be manually converted as part of our Enterprise solution.

👉 If you're interested in seeing an Enterprise demo, [get in touch](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
 with us.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/templates#can-you-add-a-new-template-for)

Can you add a new template for \_\_\_\_ ?

Yes, we'll be adding more templates over time and are taking requests. [Contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
 if you have specific suggestions.

[PreviousLanguages](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/languages)
[NextCustom templates (beta)](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Use a prompt | Plus Guide

**Using a prompt** is the easiest way to create a new presentation with Plus AI. In this mode, you enter in a short description, and Plus AI will create a content outline — which you can customize — followed by the entire presentation.

If you already know exactly what you want, try [**Upload a file**](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file)
 or [**Slide by slide**](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/slide-by-slide)
 mode instead.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/use-a-prompt#how-to-use-a-prompt)

How to use a prompt


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Launch the Plus add-on in Google Slides or PowerPoint.

Click on **New presentation** and then **Use a prompt**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FSSYh1JVDCIA18PthrYSz%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.20.00%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D897e5fd2-05e7-4c72-9479-50dc7bf5df7b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=297546a3&sv=2)

Alternatively, you can select a template and then select **Use a prompt**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fb3q2zl4MVUPRIygAUdLY%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.40.42%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D480266ba-1b9d-476a-a125-a22fef2d3af2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=108dbc0c&sv=2)

Selecting **Use a prompt** mode after choosing a template

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/use-a-prompt#write-a-prompt)

Write a prompt

Add a short description of the presentation you want to generate, or use or customize one of our presets.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F4wEZxSGxPUsZfVU1Fj0m%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.47.36%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc8af767b-153e-4c1d-bfe1-4c8dc52f7269&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=84ff6b58&sv=2)

Customizing the online course preset

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/use-a-prompt#other-options)

Other options

*   **Language:** This is the output language that your presentation will be written in. (Your prompt can be in a different language.) [Learn more about languages.](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/languages)
    
*   **Number of slides:** This is the length of the presentation. Our AI model can only handle about 20 slides right now. If you need a much longer presentation, we recommend generating one chapter at a time. Newly generated slides are appended to existing ones.
    
*   **Include Plus tips:** These are additional suggestions on generated slides. If you uncheck this box, we will not include them on your presentation.
    
*   **Custom instructions:** You can save context about you or your company instead of typing it every time. [Learn more about custom instructions.](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/custom-instructions)
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FxZIhiSOLQtPOMNyRpzcm%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.48.22%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5d215fd8-6bbc-4353-a479-217dcc065fd2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d3c879b&sv=2)

Settings

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/use-a-prompt#how-to-write-a-good-prompt)

How to write a good prompt

Here are some quick tips. You can read more on our [blog](https://www.plusdocs.com/blog/how-to-write-an-effective-ai-prompt)
.

*   Include context about the type of presentation and audience.
    
*   In addition to the overall topic, you can also ask for specific content to be included.
    

Remember you can always use text to presentation and slide-by-slide mode if you need more control than a short prompt.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FxLP6codXCMTeRTeWk0k4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De401db76-6970-4fac-afad-e00b8a1377e0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=894992ba&sv=2)

Save this cheatsheet for writing a good AI prompt.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/use-a-prompt#customize-the-outline)

Customize the outline

Based on your prompt, Plus AI will generate an outline. You can customize the outline by editing the slide titles and deleting slides.

If you don't like the outline, you can also retry this step.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FsmBOl07t7jcZNsVnj1di%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.52.53%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc61fe18e-2eb9-4109-80a1-a6768f35792a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1a3a1828&sv=2)

Reviewing and editing the outline

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/use-a-prompt#generate-slides)

Generate slides

When you're happy with your outline, Plus AI will proceed by generating the slides in your presentation.

If you did not start from a template, you can choose a presentation **theme**. Themes allow you to choose the visual look and feel of your slides, including fonts and colors. Pro users can create and save [custom themes](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding)
.

Newly generated slides are added to the end of your presentation. If you didn't start with a blank file, scroll down to find your new slides.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FUc2ROeNoqlN8edSTkCdf%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.54.01%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D532a1efe-3680-499a-a325-618f51f01bd9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f735cb2c&sv=2)

When your presentation is generated, the Plus AI generate window will close. You can keep editing with Plus.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/use-a-prompt#editing-your-presentation)

Editing your presentation

After your presentation is created, the add-on will close automatically.

At this point, your slides work just like any other Google Slides (or PowerPoint slides). You can edit them directly, share them, or export them as a PDF or other file types.

The Edit with Plus AI sidebar will open automatically to help you continue to refine your deck.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/use-a-prompt#learn-more-about-editing-with-plus-ai)

Learn more about editing with Plus AI

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/rewrite-slides)

![Cover](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FetbuS1hqd4pQEy72HSAC%252Frewrite.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De01ceecf-ed7e-46a3-9670-fc24dd20429f&width=245&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8fcfeca1&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/use-a-prompt#rewrite-content)

# Custom branding | Plus Guide

Custom branding requires a **Team plan**. [Learn more about pricing](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing)
.

You can set up custom branding to change colors, fonts, and add a logo to your slides.

Your custom brand is shared [across your team](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-for-teams)
 and can be used when [generating a presentation](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation)
, [inserting a slide](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide)
, or [remixing an existing slide](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/remix-slides)
.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#set-up-custom-branding)

Set up custom branding


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Launch the Plus add-on in Google Slides or PowerPoint. In Google Slides, go to New Presentation. In PowerPoint, click on the New Presentation button.

*   In Google Slides, click on **Custom templates** then scroll down to **Custom branding**.
    
*   In PowerPoint, Click on **Custom branding**.
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fext5j0ZvJQ9PrFabsEeQ%252FCleanShot%25202024-09-30%2520at%252014.42.13%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D671066d7-75e3-47d4-a53f-423d2c5581fb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4c735016&sv=2)

Setting up custom branding in the Plus AI add-on in Google slides or PowerPoint

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#choose-your-brand-colors)

Choose your brand colors

The vast majority of Plus AI's designs only use **primary background**, **primary text**, and **accent 1**.

If you don't have additional brand colors that should be incorporated, just set both of your primary and secondary colors to the same value. Similarly, repeat your accent colors if you don't need all 4 slots.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#select-your-fonts)

Select your fonts

Title fonts apply to titles, section headings, and other large, featured text elements. The body font is used everywhere else.

Google Slides and PowerPoint fonts are not compatible with each other, so if you want to use your custom brand in both tools, you will need to select two different set of fonts.

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#a-note-about-custom-fonts)

A note about custom fonts

You cannot use custom fonts in Google Slides (this is a Google limitation.) If you need a Google Font that is not available in the Plus dropdown, [let us know](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
 and we can add it for you.

In PowerPoint, you can use any custom font that is installed on your computer. However, the font name you enter must exactly match the one that is installed. Custom fonts may not render correctly if you share the file with others or open it in Microsoft 365 in your browser.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#add-a-logo)

Add a logo

Upload a logo if you'd like it to appear on every slide.

⚠️ Only **.jpeg**, **.png**, and **.gif** file types are supported. Use a file converter if you need.

Make sure your logo's background is transparent (or matches the slide background color) and that there is minimal whitespace around the logo itself.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#saving-your-custom-branding)

Saving your custom branding

Click save to finish setting up your custom branding.

Anyone on your team can edit your custom branding at any time. Your custom branding is shared across your organization.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#using-your-custom-branding)

Using your custom branding


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can select your custom branding as a separate "template" when generating a new presentation.

You can use select your custom brand in the template dropdown when [inserting a slide](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide)
, or [remixing an existing slide](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/remix-slides)
.

Currently, the layout thumbnails in the Insert and Remix tabs do not update when you select your custom brand. But don't worry, your custom theme will be applied to your generated slide.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#custom-branding-faqs)

Custom branding FAQs


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

What if I don't have multiple text (or background or accent) colors?[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#what-if-i-dont-have-multiple-text-or-background-or-accent-colors)

Just set both the primary and secondary text (or background) colors to the same value.

You can also repeat accent colors. If you only have one, just set all 4 accent colors to the same value.

How can I preview my custom branding?[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#how-can-i-preview-my-custom-branding)

We're working on adding better previews for custom branding. In the meantime, just generate a quick presentation to see what it will look like.

How can I upload a custom font to Google Slides?[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#how-can-i-upload-a-custom-font-to-google-slides)

Unfortunately Google Slides (not Plus) does not support custom fonts. Your best bet is to select a Google Font that comes close.

I need a Google Font that is not available in the dropdown[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#i-need-a-google-font-that-is-not-available-in-the-dropdown)

[Send us a note](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
 and we can add it for you.

Why can't I upload my logo as an SVG?[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#why-cant-i-upload-my-logo-as-an-svg)

Google Slides sadly does not support SVGs at all. Use an image converter to save your logo as a transparent png instead.

Can I apply my custom branding to one of the other Plus templates?[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#can-i-apply-my-custom-branding-to-one-of-the-other-plus-templates)

Unfortunately not right now. However, we can custom design a template for you with a lot more flexibility. [Contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
 about an Enterprise plan if you're interested.

How do I upload my existing company template?[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#how-do-i-upload-my-existing-company-template)

Unfortunately you can't. Custom templates are only available for Enterprise customers.

A normal Google Slides or PowerPoint template doesn't work with our AI designer out-of-the box.

We have to convert your slide library into a format that our AI models can understand and then teach our AI models to design slides that fit your needs. This takes a week or two.

[Contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
 if you're interested in an Enterprise plan.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#learn-more)

Learn more


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide)

![Cover](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FZZa8hd5YTNqqcoRAwGfe%252Fgenerate%2520presentation%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D03eb10e2-7473-462a-94f4-fa79cd3901d3&width=245&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98e0b4d1&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding#generate-a-new-presentation)

Generate a new presentation

Insert a single slide

![Cover](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F0gdVWuKCiGM4KT9iYmjo%252Fremix%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D79ea82fc-026f-499e-b43b-f59e73e8c510&width=245&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ad905712&sv=2)

# Take a Snapshot | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/take-a-snapshot#what-is-a-snapshot)

What is a Snapshot?

A "Snapshot" is a screenshot that Plus can automatically take for you, over and over, on a schedule or on demand.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/take-a-snapshot#taking-a-snapshot)

Taking a Snapshot

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FL4TimGQ8dGD4GQw3d0Yh%252FSnapshot%2520capture.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D543f6b00-78a7-4a19-afa6-73bd3aba6022&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=41d61f03&sv=2)

Taking a Snapshot with the Plus browser extension

You can take a Snapshot of virtually any site or app that you can access in a browser.

1.  Navigate to the page with the dashboard or chart you want to capture.
    
2.  Open the Plus extension and click on "Take a Snapshot." Or use the Shift + Cmd + S shortcut (Shift + Ctrl + S on Windows)
    
3.  A new window will pop up where you can take the Snapshot.
    
4.  Scroll to the chart or area you want to capture. Click and drag to draw a box to capture your Snapshot, just like taking a screenshot.
    

On [some apps and sites](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/sites-with-smart-capture)
, we also highlight the most commonly captured content and offer a one click capture option. These elements will be outlined in blue and you can click "Take Snapshot" to capture them. [Learn more](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/sites-with-smart-capture)
 about smart capture

Your Snapshot is now queued and will be processed automatically. You can immediately rename your Snapshot or change how often it automatically refreshes. You can also take another Snapshot on the same page or close this recording window.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/take-a-snapshot#where-are-the-snapshots-ive-taken)

Where are the Snapshots I've taken?

As soon as you take a Snapshot, it will appear in your extension and app in a pending state. It can take up to a minute for a Snapshot to finish processing.

You can find your most recent Snapshots in the extension to easily check whether the capture was good. You can also copy the [share link](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share/share-links)
, refresh the Snapshot, or delete it.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FS7Ryaub1rm6hEPIZh0oR%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-24%2520at%252012.47.57%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D833ddc25-4a35-4770-bc66-4ddc0b0b9df3&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3c54b8fb&sv=2)

Learn more: [Snapshots](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots)

[PreviousSet up Plus](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/set-up-plus)
[NextCreate a Page](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/create-a-page)

Last updated 11 months ago

# Snapshot settings | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-settings#snapshot-settings)

Snapshot settings

You can show and hide the Snapshot settings panel from the top toolbar.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F1PRs6vHzP4ptiInfx8t4%252FCleanShot%25202022-11-23%2520at%252014.06.54%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd84a54c2-3307-4418-b7e6-a7d3c52e2182&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1b9503e7&sv=2)

Show or hide the Snapshot settings panel

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-settings#refreshing-a-snapshot)

Refreshing a Snapshot

You can set a schedule on which a Snapshot will automatically update, or leave it on "manual." Either way, you can refresh a Snapshot manually whenever you'd like, by clicking **Refresh Snapshot**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FO54QQm9BoRUBbQemSIpl%252FCleanShot%25202022-11-23%2520at%252014.08.59%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df2f1b9fc-1a59-493a-b3f2-952c5129c85f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b04bbce6&sv=2)

Updating the refresh rate of a Snapshot or triggering a manual refresh

You can also refresh Snapshots directly from [Google Slides](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace)
, [Slack](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack)
, and [embeds in other apps](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps)
 like Notion or Coda.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-settings#repair-snapshot)

Repair Snapshot

Occasionally, your Snapshots will need manual intervention to continue refreshing properly. For example, most apps will prompt you to log back in every couple of weeks, so your Snapshots also need to be logged back in on the same schedule. Other times, if the underlying app changes, you may need to recapture the Snapshot because the chart has moved.

Plus will attempt to detect these issues when they happen and notify you to repair your Snapshots.

[Snapshot repair](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-repair)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-settings#source)

Source

The source link is the URL where the Snapshot was taken. This is a great way to quickly jump to the underlying data if you have additional questions or want to do more exploration.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F3NKwsoHITQRahcFhGOJL%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-22%2520at%252017.10.34.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8eaf07ad-52ff-4b59-9cf4-57fe499a6753&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e774d06d&sv=2)

Use the source link to quickly jump into the underlying data

[PreviousSites with smart capture](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/sites-with-smart-capture)
[NextSnapshot versions](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-versions)

Last updated 2 years ago

# Edit documents | Plus Guide

Plus AI can help you revise, rewrite, or even translate existing text in your Google Docs.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-google-docs/edit-documents#launch-edit-with-plus-ai)

Launch Edit with Plus AI


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a [new Google Doc](http://docs.new/)
 or open an existing one, then launch the Plus add-on from the Extensions menu: **Extensions** > **Plus AI** > **Edit with Plus AI**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F1pGHFopGTibj32QgU23I%252FCleanShot%25202024-02-06%2520at%252016.26.47%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0e08395c-4187-43ea-ba85-623a64b3ade0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3ef6433c&sv=2)

Open the Plus AI extension in Google Docs

Navigate to the **Edit** tab.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fbivf6nSIaWFzrScZ9Xit%252FCleanShot%25202024-02-06%2520at%252016.44.37%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D346024cb-1d50-4a20-b512-5439dc25c175&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=24e889a4&sv=2)

Select the text you want to rewrite

Enter a prompt or use one of our presets.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FtGkPiGpPifwnp6Q5vV9Y%252FCleanShot%25202024-02-06%2520at%252016.47.48%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D756d1900-d7c4-4f22-9857-5b4542d98044&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=40c69abc&sv=2)

Then click Generate. This usually takes a few seconds, but can take up to a minute or so for more complex content.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-google-docs/edit-documents#undo-and-redo)

Undo and redo


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use the native undo and redo actions in Google Docs on any Plus AI insertions or edits.

To undo, click the button in the Google Docs toolbar or press ⌘Z (or Ctrl + Z) on your keyboard.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FeydMMHPiTaeXMaNVwvyp%252FCleanShot%25202024-02-06%2520at%252016.36.46%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2952b87d-9aa8-4739-8bb4-327120de8537&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9aeb2801&sv=2)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-google-docs/edit-documents#text-formatting)

Text formatting


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

While Plus AI can do basic formatting (paragraph breaks, headers, bullets and lists), it cannot do more advanced formatting, like changing colors or fonts, or add media like images or videos.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-google-docs/edit-documents#translating-text)

Translating text


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Select the section you want to translate (you can select the entire document if you want), and use the Translate preset prompt.

Use the language dropdown to select the language you want to translate _**to**_ (Plus AI will automatically detect the language you're translating _from_). Make sure you select the language instead of putting it in the prompt.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FsiYc4lUx52oSHk394RhH%252FCleanShot%25202024-02-06%2520at%252016.50.37%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b34f8dc-b308-458b-99d7-bd7914a5192f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=65d85123&sv=2)

[PreviousGenerate a new document](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-google-docs/generate-a-new-document)
[NextContact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)

# Set up Plus | Plus Guide

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/set-up-plus#creating-an-account)

Creating an account


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Go to [app.plusdocs.com/register](https://app.plusdocs.com/register)
 to create an account.

After you sign up, you will be prompted to join an existing organization or to create a new one.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/set-up-plus#logging-into-the-web-app)

Logging into the web app

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FiSZhUMqFtUTn3NBRoFO4%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-23%2520at%252016.34.50%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db9f3f949-4f7a-459d-85aa-e0ac25ce3ce6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5991b0f7&sv=2)

You can find all your Snapshots and Pages in the web app

The web app is where you will find all the Snapshots you have taken. New Snapshots appear in Drafts by default. The Team space is content that is shared across your organization.

Access the web app at [app.plusdocs.com](https://app.plusdocs.com/)
 from any web browser, including your mobile device.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/set-up-plus#installing-the-chrome-extension)

Installing the chrome extension


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You need the Chrome extension to take Snapshots. If you only plan to use Plus to view Snapshots other team members have taken, you do not need the extension.

Go to the [Plus extension in the Chrome store](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/plus/bnebanooamokkihfjepphafoekheipfh)
. Click the **Add to Chrome** button to install the extension. Then log into your Plus account.

We recommend "pinning" the extension so it is accessible for taking new Snapshots.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FjH3zEumUaufCMs70iIXS%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-24%2520at%252012.00.07.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7b12e78-bfbf-44ea-b5cb-3a96c124ef72&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=efa193a0&sv=2)

Pin the Plus extension for ease of access

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/set-up-plus#browser-support-for-the-extension)

Browser support for the extension

The extension is designed to be used with Google Chrome.

It will also work for other chromium-based browsers, including Microsoft Edge, Brave, and Arc.

The browser extension does not work on mobile devices, though you can view all the Snapshots you've captured on your phone in our web app.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/set-up-plus#bookmark-the-web-app)

Bookmark the web app


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can bookmark [app.plusdocs.com](https://app.plusdocs.com/)
 for easy access.

You can also always navigate to the web app by clicking on the Plus logo in the extension.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/set-up-plus#bookmark-the-web-app-on-your-mobile-device)

Bookmark the web app on your mobile device

You can access all your content in the Plus web app from any mobile device. This is a great way to quickly review data on your phone without logging into any tools.

For quick access, we recommend bookmarking the Plus web app on your phone.

iOS/Safari

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/set-up-plus#tab-ios-safari)

Android/Chrome

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/set-up-plus#tab-android-chrome)

Go to app.plusdocs.com in Safari.

Tap the Share icon.

Choose "Add to Homescreen."

Open app.plusdocs.com in Chrome.

Tap the menu icon (three dots).

Choose "Add to Homescreen."

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/set-up-plus#set-up-plus-with-your-other-tools)

Set up Plus with your other tools


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Plus is designed to work with your existing collaboration tools:

*   Install the [Plus for Google Slides](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace)
     add-on to add Snapshots to your Google Slides presentations and easily refresh them as needed.
    
*   Install the [Plus app for Slack](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack)
     to share Plus Snapshots and Pages more easily in your workspace.
    
*   [Embed Plus content](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps)
     in other document editors and apps, like Notion and Confluence.
    

[PreviousStart Guide](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide)
[NextTake a Snapshot](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/take-a-snapshot)

# Upload a file | Plus Guide

Uploading a file requires a **Pro or Team plan**. [Learn more about pricing](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing)
.

Use this mode if you want to transform **existing content** into a presentation. You can either upload a file or paste in plain text.

This mode is useful for creating presentations from proprietary information (e.g., a paper you've written) or current events — like other AI tools, Plus does not have knowledge of the latest news.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file#how-to-upload-a-file)

How to upload a file


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Launch Plus AI in [Google Slides](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides)
 or [PowerPoint](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint)
.

Click on **New presentation** and then **Upload a file**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FQWMbTN0KmG33o668bmm9%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.20.00%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71c7a369-45cc-4625-ad68-7cdebfb4c024&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4d5f45ce&sv=2)

Selecting **Upload a file** mode in Plus

Alternatively, you can select a template and then select **Upload a file**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FTTf2n0takgahcMVYgWXs%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.40.42%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da17116da-05a4-4008-a790-2c1820506a6e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=29af696a&sv=2)

Selecting **Upload a file** mode after choosing a template

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file#upload-a-file)

Upload a file

Click choose file to select your file. You can upload a PDF, .docx (Word Document), .pptx (PowerPoint), or .txt (text file). If your file type isn't available, use **Paste in text** instead.

Currently, Plus AI cannot extract images, diagrams, or charts from your document.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FmEgrzlnZosouQck9ZNQR%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.59.19%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7d01698c-a570-4517-85f9-eeace3697460&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=82fc26e2&sv=2)

Selecting a file to upload

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file#paste-in-content)

Paste in content

In **Upload a file** mode, click on the **Paste in text** button.

Paste in an article, document, or other text. Adding images is not yet supported (remember, you can always add them directly to the slides later).

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FHJk2cQypSz4DAUlLdR6Q%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252016.02.53%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D577c8e69-c193-4681-b55a-75955ad2f357&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9d420b6e&sv=2)

Click on **Paste in text** if your file format isn't supported.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FLFrEB9UASDxWDv8iWUQJ%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252016.05.21%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7ef03bf7-ebea-4e41-97db-caccda66da1d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28f2c6f1&sv=2)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file#enhance-vs-preserve)

Enhance vs Preserve

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FcTxjK88zTJXf9PgykeKR%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252016.06.48%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dacc67740-2c97-41d5-8226-e7310b226f18&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5fa7ea76&sv=2)

Enhance vs preserve setting

Choose **Enhance** if you want Plus to rewrite your content to better fit the presentation format. For example, use this if you're uploading a meeting transcript that needs cleanup.

Choose **Preserve** if you want Plus to use as much verbatim text from your document as possible. Plus will try to quote directly from your document, but will avoid elaborating or summarizing.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file#other-settings)

Other settings

*   **Language:** This is the output language that your presentation will be written in. (Your prompt can be in a different language.) [Learn more about languages.](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/languages)
    
*   **Number of slides:** This is the length of the presentation. Our AI model can only handle about 20 slides right now. If you need a much longer presentation, we recommend generating one chapter at a time. Newly generated slides are appended to existing ones.
    
*   **Include Plus tips:** These are additional suggestions on generated slides. If you uncheck this box, we will not include them on your presentation.
    
*   **Custom instructions:** You can save context about you or your company instead of typing it every time. [Learn more about custom instructions.](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/custom-instructions)
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FnLoMLZppBmu2MWE6bHKv%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.59.22%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd4452cf-9eab-448b-b635-0a80834e1296&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d981accb&sv=2)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file#editing-your-presentation)

Editing your presentation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After your presentation is created, the add-on will close automatically.

Newly generated slides are added to the end of your presentation. If you didn't start with a blank file, scroll down to find your new slides.

At this point, your slides work just like any other Google Slides (or PowerPoint slides). You can edit them directly, share them, or export them as a PDF or other file type.

The **Edit with Plus AI** sidebar will open automatically to help you continue to refine your deck.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FUc2ROeNoqlN8edSTkCdf%252FCleanShot%25202024-04-17%2520at%252015.54.01%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D532a1efe-3680-499a-a325-618f51f01bd9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f735cb2c&sv=2)

When your presentation is generated, the Plus AI generate window will close. You can keep editing with Plus.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file#learn-more-about-editing-with-plus-ai)

Learn more about editing with Plus AI

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/rewrite-slides)

![Cover](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FetbuS1hqd4pQEy72HSAC%252Frewrite.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De01ceecf-ed7e-46a3-9670-fc24dd20429f&width=245&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8fcfeca1&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file#rewrite-content)

Rewrite content

Change the tone or audience

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide)

![Cover](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FBTJg752HnsOs1i9Hs0og%252Finsert.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D679eae78-bc52-4cba-b147-2609b2f39308&width=245&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=754ab5b&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file#insert-a-single-slide)

Insert a single slide

Great for editing existing presentations

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/remix-slides)

# Generate images with AI | Plus Guide

Inserting images with AI requires a Pro or **Team** plan. [Learn more about pricing.](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-plans-and-billing)

When you generate a [new presentation](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation)
, Plus automatically adds AI-generated images to your slides, where appropriate. (💡**Pro-tip:** You can add instructions like "include lots of images" to your prompt if you want a more image-heavy presentation.)

When editing an existing presentation, you can generate individual AI images for your slides for more control and variation.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-images-with-ai#launch-edit-with-plus-ai)

Launch Edit with Plus AI


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Google Slides[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-images-with-ai#google-slides)

Launch Google Slides (Here is a shortcut: [https://slides.new](https://slides.new/)
).

In Google Slides, go to **Extensions** > **Plus AI for Google Slides** > **Edit with Plus AI**.

In the Plus AI sidebar, click on **Edit with AI** and select **Generate images**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fko9MlfUsetIYXIUPxFgu%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-14%2520at%252010.02.15%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5e02c22-8a3f-4df7-9b1e-62a786fecf9f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=85277175&sv=2)

**Troubleshooting:**

*   If you don't see Plus AI in the Extensions menu, make sure you have it [installed](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides)
    .
    
*   If you don't see any options under Plus AI (except "Help"), reload the page in your browser and give it a minute to load.
    
*   Check out our [troubleshooting guide](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting)
    .
    

PowerPoint[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-images-with-ai#powerpoint)

In PowerPoint, go to the **Home** tab of the menu > **Add-ins** \> **Plus AI**. (Search for Plus AI if it does not appear)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F5I8hq5Odi9SmhlwkeeFG%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-13%2520at%252014.48.13%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44b1143f-3ff6-4997-b1fc-79be41aec12d&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7cd26334&sv=2)

In the Plus AI sidebar, click on **Edit with AI** and select **Generate images**.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-images-with-ai#generate-images)

Generate images


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the Plus AI sidebar, click the **Edit with AI** dropdown and select **Generate images**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FulNcPB1zKBS6aIGPYQQt%252FCleanShot%25202024-12-02%2520at%252010.33.10%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d18bdea-12ff-4f64-bb7d-e55a2e8f0518&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=68973186&sv=2)

Launching the Generate images feature

Add a prompt, select an image style if you'd like, and click **Insert new image**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FUPplh0mufQcPyGCqR4Fy%252FCleanShot%25202024-12-02%2520at%252010.41.18%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0be49327-af29-4f91-8150-4606bd110223&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db50d3d9&sv=2)

Inserting an AI generated image with Plus AI

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-images-with-ai#using-a-style-preset)

Using a style preset

Use the provided style presets for the best results. You can toggle between Photography and Illustration in the **Medium** dropdown.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FwSd81UouTfG2MQ714J7R%252FCleanShot%25202024-12-02%2520at%252010.43.52%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9b966a7c-34f5-4294-82f5-b103ca758355&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ec340fbc&sv=2)

Choose between Photography and Illustration presets

Click on an image style thumbnail to select it. Click again to deselect it.

If your presentation was generated from a Plus AI template, the style preset that was used for your presentation will be automatically selected when you launch the Edit with Plus sidebar.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F5k5J03ttyyQ6DRhJ3Arr%252FCleanShot%25202024-12-02%2520at%252011.01.07%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D934b795f-0f58-4b45-988a-2338824ddb34&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=37e4b060&sv=2)

Examples of different AI photography style presets, using the same prompt

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-images-with-ai#how-to-write-a-good-image-prompt)

How to write a good image prompt

*   Describe the contents of the image directly. Use specific, concrete descriptions.
    
*   Omit words and phrases like "image of" or "illustration of."
    
*   The sweet spot for an image description is 2-3 sentences. Too much detail can lead to confusing results.
    

Here's an example of a good image prompt:

> an astronaut standing on a barren, moon-like surface. The astronaut is dressed in an orange spacesuit with a helmet and a large backpack, facing to the right.

Not all style presets will work equally well with all prompts, so experiment with a few different ones if you're not getting a good result.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-images-with-ai#when-should-i-not-use-ai-generated-images)

When should I not use AI generated images?

As you can expect, there are scenarios where AI generated images don't work as well. Here are some examples where we recommend not using AI images:

*   Photographs of real people (e.g., historical figures, celebrities)
    
*   Maps, scientific diagrams, and other schematics where accuracy is important
    
*   Charts and graphs
    
*   Images that contain words (e.g., signs, names, phrases)
    

For these types of assets, we recommend using internet images instead.

Conveniently, since Plus AI works directly inside of Google Slides and PowerPoint, it's easy to replace images manually — just treat the slide like any other file in Google Slide or PowerPoint.

[PreviousPrompt presets](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/prompt-presets)
[NextGenerate a new document](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-google-docs/generate-a-new-document)

# Snapshot versions | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-versions#what-are-snapshot-versions)

What are Snapshot versions

Every time Plus refreshes a Snapshot, a new version is created. You can see all the previous versions of a Snapshot in the timeline.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FWYTR6MggwEGXFoDxF7ff%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-23%2520at%252015.34.03%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D741ba8cb-40c1-4a73-9e3c-6b4bb62bb8a3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=803f40a8&sv=2)

Snapshot versions

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-versions#sharing-versions)

Sharing versions

You can share a specific version of a Snapshot by selecting in the Snapshot viewer, clicking share, and then checking the option to "Share only this version." This can be useful for pointing the viewer to a specific point-in-time, like highlighting something that happened last week.

Learn more: [Share links](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share/share-links)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FPzAdTogZAsGWTvs2V2b9%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-23%2520at%252015.35.00%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D690f742e-e57e-4595-bc50-d140b2c01540&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8864b200&sv=2)

Copying the URL for a specific Snapshot version

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-versions#using-versions-on-pages)

Using versions on Pages

When you place a Snapshot on a Page, by default, the Page will always show the latest version of a Snapshot. You can also choose to show a specific version of a Snapshot, which will not update automatically.

To select a specific version, select a Snapshot on a Page, then click on the version you want to display in the timeline.

You can use add two different versions of the same Snapshot to a Page in order to compare two different time frames.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FoPryl8ft83kE1kgibt7K%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-23%2520at%252015.41.13%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94ddb701-9154-4fd6-89c2-396666ea30e0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f999e3d3&sv=2)

Using different versions of the same Snapshot on a Page to compare different time frames

[PreviousSnapshot settings](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-settings)
[NextConnections](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/connections)

# Share with others | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/share-with-others#ways-to-share-content)

Ways to share content

You can share your Snapshots and Pages with someone else in multiple ways:

1.  Invite them to your Team
    
2.  Share a view-only link to a specific piece of content
    
3.  Use an integration to share Plus content using other collaboration tools
    

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/share-with-others#inviting-someone-to-your-organization)

Inviting someone to your Organization

This is the best way to share content with your immediate team, coworkers, and other internal stakeholders. Organization members have shared access to Snapshots and Pages in a Team space.

You can use the Team space to do things like create a shared folder of metrics you review weekly as a team, give visibility to your coworker who doesn't have access to the same tools you do, and allow an executive to quickly access important data from their phone.

Learn more: Organizations

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/share-with-others#share-a-view-only-link)

Share a view-only link

If you only want to to share a specific piece of content with someone without allowing them to edit or refresh that Snapshot or Page, use the share link. This is a great way to share a specific set of information with a third party who shouldn't have access to the underlying app.

Share links can be private, public, or passcode protected. You can always update this setting later if you want to revoke access, for example.

Learn more: [Share links](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share/share-links)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/share-with-others#use-plus-content-in-other-collaboration-tools)

Use Plus content in other collaboration tools

When you share Plus content using other tools, you can take advantage of the collaboration features and permissions/controls those other tools provide. For example, you can collaborate on a Google slides presentation or Notion document together with other teammates.

Learn more about the [Plus add-on for Google Slides and Docs](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace)
, [embedding Plus in other apps](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps)
, and [sharing Plus content in Slack](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack)
.

We're working on other integrations with communication and collaboration tools. If there is a specific one that is top-of-mind for you, [let us know](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

[PreviousCreate a Page](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/create-a-page)
[NextChrome extension](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/chrome-extension)

Last updated 11 months ago
