# Updating the extension | Plus Guide

We regularly make updates to Plus to introduce new features and improve reliability, to ensure that you have a smooth Snapshot-taking experience. Your browser will keep your Plus extension up-to-date automatically.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/chrome-extension/updating-the-extension#checking-which-version-of-plus-you-have-installed)

Checking which version of Plus you have installed

By default, your browser will keep the Plus extension up to date automatically. You generally do not need to manually update the extension. However, there are occasionally times where it may be helpful to our support team to determine which version of the extension you have installed, in case you are running into an issue while trying to capture a Snapshot.

To access your browser extension settings in Google Chrome, follow these steps:

Click on the three dot menu in the top right of your browser, then navigate down to "More tools", followed by clicking on "Extensions".

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F9wdv28KyfNB17arQBSde%252FCleanShot%25202023-01-20%2520at%252009.16.44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd105b6b-5b1c-4762-99b6-241b05a521fa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94bc733b&sv=2)

This may look slightly different if you are using another browser, such as Microsoft Edge or Arc. Contact our support team if you need assistance with these browsers.

On the extensions page, click on the "Details" button on the Plus extension.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FLxBoDEMkis3rNLWziKR6%252FCleanShot%25202023-01-20%2520at%252009.20.00.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6cdbfbb9-e95a-4bca-acd4-b6b4362811f0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=57bf94f3&sv=2)

On this screen, you will see what version of the extension you have installed. Let our support team know this version number, and they can help you determine if you have the latest version installed.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FksiwaoX2uNXFiAFfVExt%252FCleanShot%25202023-01-20%2520at%252009.20.47.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dce8270d0-a3b2-4f6b-91aa-e8b062f0b0f2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5a1eca27&sv=2)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/chrome-extension/updating-the-extension#manually-updating-your-extension)

Manually updating your extension

Your browser should keep Plus up-to-date automatically. However, there are occasions where a browser may not have automatically updated our extension. This can be due to a variety of factors, that are outside of Plus' control. The most common reason is that an update is still in progress of being rolled out to all users by Google. In general, we aim to keep our systems compatible with old versions of the extension.

If you would like to manually check for updates, or our support team has asked you to do so, here's how you can easily check for updates on your extensions:

Click on the three dot menu in the top right of your browser, then navigate down to "More tools", followed by clicking on "Extensions".

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FAgRys4oVNtM6Xegqyo4T%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e567c31-e832-4da6-bfdd-eb275a7bde27&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d84c371&sv=2)

This may look slightly different if you are using another browser, such as Microsoft Edge or Arc. Contact our support team if you need assistance with these browsers.

At the top right of the page, enable the toggle for "Developer mode". We'll only need to turn this on temporarily, and it will not affect any of your other extensions or web pages.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FZFXZtHiG4tGoF56VYe8T%252FCleanShot%25202023-01-20%2520at%252009.25.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4920e408-d055-4dfd-a6ba-d231cdcfe6a4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d16e7f38&sv=2)

A new set of buttons should have appeared at the left of your screen. Click the button that says "Update", underneath the "Extensions" header at the top left.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fv1qY19yvXLTUAbaBlppm%252FCleanShot%25202023-01-20%2520at%252009.26.44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D068b1999-70e8-48ce-ab0b-8cd57b747771&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=554219c1&sv=2)

After you click on this button, wait about 30 seconds. You may see the version number of the Plus extension increase, if there was an update. Once updates have completed, finish the process by turning off "Developer mode" at the top right of the page.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F4w5sCvu55udSOqP5Fq1v%252FCleanShot%25202023-01-20%2520at%252009.28.26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D00e92878-2a5a-4bd0-ab03-30a6b9a6bc4f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=46a4b9d7&sv=2)

[PreviousChrome extension](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/chrome-extension)
[NextSnapshots](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Troubleshooting | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#general-issues)

General issues

I upgraded but I'm still seeing limits in Plus AI[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#i-upgraded-but-im-still-seeing-limits-in-plus-ai)

1.  Reload the Plus extension.
    
    *   In Google Slides, reload your browser page and then relaunch Plus AI.
        
    *   In PowerPoint, close and relaunch the add-in.
        
    
2.  If you're on the **Basic** plan, note that some of our paid features are limited to the higher **Pro** and **Team** tiers. Check our [pricing page](https://www.plusdocs.com/pricing)
     to make sure you are on the correct plan.
    
3.  Make sure you are signed into the correct account. You can verify your email in the dropdown menu of the add-on.
    
4.  Make sure you are using the correct [organization](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-for-teams)
     — **remember that paid subscriptions are tied to a specific org**. You can see which org you're a member of an switch to the correct one in the same dropdown menu in the add-on.
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fydl44uEuLXh8MVMe9dve%252FCleanShot%25202025-06-30%2520at%252016.23.43%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D084f83ec-1a82-49d3-b8dc-5ca7af349361&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=35ac8c97&sv=2)

I'm signed into the wrong account[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#im-signed-into-the-wrong-account)

To switch accounts, open the add-on in Google Slides or PowerPoint, open the dropdown menu and click **log out**. You can also verify which email you are logged into.

This menu also allows you to switch between [multiple organizations](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/plus-ai-for-teams)
 — remember that a paid subscription is tied to a specific org, so make sure you're in the correct one to access Plus AI features.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FBc4CGXReQoegT6viKomx%252FCleanShot%25202025-06-30%2520at%252016.23.43%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea0e72df-bebd-4c8e-ae5a-83d715229b42&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4f8aeebf&sv=2)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#google-slides-installation-issues)

Google Slides installation issues

Plus AI isn't loading in Google Slides[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#plus-ai-isnt-loading-in-google-slides)

"_I've installed the Plus AI add-on, but the only option I see in the Extensions menu under Plus AI is Help."_

*   Disable active browser extensions.
    
*   Try reloading the page and relaunching the extensions menu.
    
*   Give it a minute to fully load.
    
*   If you don't see the Plus AI add-on at all under your Extensions menu, make sure it is [installed](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-google-slides)
    .
    

Sometimes the extension can take a second or two to load properly, especially if you're on a slower connection. During this time, the only option in the extensions menu is "Help."

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FuhVoi06otiEvjPQmzXSH%252Fextensionmenutroubleshooting.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd396d15e-33e4-47b7-bfe9-bacd8b9cd4ae&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e91e9e02&sv=2)

Sometimes the Google Slides extensions menu is finicky

Plus AI is telling me I can't use multiple Google accounts[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#plus-ai-is-telling-me-i-cant-use-multiple-google-accounts)

_"When I launch the Plus AI extension, I see an error that I can't use multiple Google accounts."_

You can use Plus AI with multiple Google accounts, you just can't be logged into both of them in the same browser.

The workaround is to set up multiple browser profiles:

*   Set up two (or more) [Chrome profiles](https://support.google.com/chrome/answer/2364824?hl=en&co=GENIE.Platform%3DDesktop)
     (or [Safari Profiles](https://support.apple.com/en-us/HT212544)
    ), e.g., one for work and one for your personal email.
    
*   Log into the respective Google account on each profile. When you want to switch between them, use the profile switcher in your browser.
    
*   In Google Slides, confirm you're only logged into the one email you want to use with Plus.
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FxcMB0hZZ5RdvxC8qaQTF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2ce169e0-905e-4714-9ee8-a88066a96bbf&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2e55a4cc&sv=2)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#powerpoint-installation-issues)

PowerPoint installation issues

I'm installing from the AppSource store and I can't login.[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#im-installing-from-the-appsource-store-and-i-cant-login)

If you have multiple Microsoft accounts, you might run into some sign in issues when trying to install AppSource apps.

We recommend [installing the add-in directly within the app.](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint)

I don't have permission to install add-ins on my work account[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#i-dont-have-permission-to-install-add-ins-on-my-work-account)

Ask your Microsoft Office admin or IT to enable the Plus AI app. [https://appsource.microsoft.com/en-us/product/office/WA200007130](https://appsource.microsoft.com/en-us/product/office/WA200007130)

Alternatively, you can use the Plus add-in with a personal Microsoft account. (Unfortunately you will need a paid Microsoft Office subscription either way.)

The add-ins button is disabled in my PowerPoint app[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#the-add-ins-button-is-disabled-in-my-powerpoint-app)

*   Make sure you have at least 1 slide in your presentation.
    
*   Make sure you are not in "slide sorter" mode (where slides are displayed as a grid of thumbnails). Switch to "normal" mode (the book icon).
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FJefkR91HUdrkQW07PcK4%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-24%2520at%252016.11.13%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D173507d5-398e-45c3-ae4b-17fc1eac8213&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6e506b19&sv=2)

You must have at least one slide and be in "Normal" mode to access the Add-ins menu

The add-in doesn't work properly in PowerPoint for the Web (in my browser)[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#the-add-in-doesnt-work-properly-in-powerpoint-for-the-web-in-my-browser)

We strongly encourage using Plus AI in the PowerPoint desktop app

Some limitations of PowerPoint in the browser mean that Plus AI generated content may not be formatted correctly. [Learn more](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint/powerpoint-desktop-app-recommended)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#generating-presentations)

Generating presentations

My presentations continuously fail to generate.[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#my-presentations-continuously-fail-to-generate)

*   Reload the add-on
    
    *   In Google Slides, reload the page in your browser, then relaunch Plus AI
        
    *   In PowerPoint, close and reload the extension
        
    
*   Try a **different prompt**
    
    *   If you've been using your own prompt, try one of the preset options
        
    *   If you're trying to upload a file, try starting from a prompt instead
        
    

If you perform these troubleshooting steps and you continue to get an error, [contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

To help us identify the problem, please include

*   The email associated with your Plus AI account
    
*   Whether you're using Google Slides or PowerPoint
    
*   All the prompt(s) / file(s) you tried that failed
    
*   Details about the error — did any prompts work? does the add-on fail immediately or after a few minutes?
    

It says I successfully generated a presentation, but I don't see it.[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#it-says-i-successfully-generated-a-presentation-but-i-dont-see-it)

*   In Google Slides, slides for a new presentation get added to the end of your presentation. Make sure you scroll down to the end of your presentation to see your new slides.
    
*   In PowerPoint, new slides are appended to the beginning of your presentation.
    

How do I generate more than 30 slides per presentation?[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#how-do-i-generate-more-than-30-slides-per-presentation)

Plus AI has a limit of 30 slides per presentation generated.

To create a longer presentation, we recommend simply breaking up your prompt into multiple chapters and generating multiple presentations (each time you do it, the new slides just get added to the presentation you have open.) You'll then need to do a little bit of work to delete the extra title and agenda slides.

I can't find a presentation I generated previously.[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#i-cant-find-a-presentation-i-generated-previously)

_"I generated a presentation with Plus AI but seem to have lost it."_

Go to the [History](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/history)
 view to find a list of your previously generated presentations.

*   **In Google Slides:** Plus AI only works on files that you have access to and can edit, so you can also find all of your generated slides in your Google Slides history: [https://slides.google.com](https://slides.google.com/)
    

*   If you deleted slides (or the presentation) after generating them, we don't retain a copy of them.
    

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#formatting)

Formatting


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Can I upload a custom font in Google Slides?[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#can-i-upload-a-custom-font-in-google-slides)

Unfortunately no. Because Plus AI works within Google Slides and Google Slides only supports Google Fonts, you cannot upload a custom font

You can use custom fonts with [custom branding](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding)
 in Plus AI for PowerPoint. We can also

Plus AI doesn't follow my formatting instructions[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#plus-ai-doesnt-follow-my-formatting-instructions)

Currently, Plus AI only works with prompts about presentation **content**, not design.

We offer a wide selection of [presentation templates](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/templates)
 to help you achieve the visual style you want. For additional customization, you can:

*   Use [custom branding](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding)
     to change fonts, colors, and add a logo.
    
*   Upload a simple [custom template](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta)
     (up to 25 slides)
    
*   [Contact us](https://plusai.com/contact-enterprise)
     about Enterprise options if you need an advanced custom template (more slides, more designs, charts/icons/diagrams)
    

I want to upload a whole presentation and use Plus to reformat it[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#i-want-to-upload-a-whole-presentation-and-use-plus-to-reformat-it)

We do not recommend using [Upload a file](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file)
 for this — that workflow is designed to synthesize a document into a new presentation, so your content will be reorganized and rewritten.

The best way to reformat slides currently is is one slide at a time using [Remix slides](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/remix-slides)
, where you can select the slide design you want and control how much your content gets rewritten.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/troubleshooting#need-more-help)

Need more help?

# Snapshots | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots#what-is-a-snapshot)

What is a Snapshot?

A "Snapshot" is a screenshot that Plus can automatically take for you, over and over, on a schedule or on demand.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots#taking-a-snapshot)

Taking a Snapshot

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FLwh7yitBVTGj9zac0K8Z%252FSnapshot%2520capture.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3290b2d5-3b58-44e4-b9c2-9ffa80c0a213&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c402485f&sv=2)

Taking a Snapshot with the Plus browser extension

You can take a Snapshot of virtually any site or app that you can access in a browser.

1.  Navigate to the page with the dashboard or chart you want to capture.
    
2.  Open the Plus extension and click on "Take a Snapshot." Or use the Shift + Cmd + S shortcut (Shift + Ctrl + S on Windows)
    
3.  A new window will pop up where you can take the Snapshot.
    
4.  Scroll to the chart or area you want to capture. Click and drag to draw a box to capture your Snapshot, just like taking a screenshot.
    

On [some apps and sites](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/sites-with-smart-capture)
, we also highlight the most commonly captured content and offer a one click capture option. These elements will be outlined in blue and you can click "Take Snapshot" to capture them.

Your Snapshot is now queued and will be processed automatically. You can immediately rename your Snapshot or change how often it automatically refreshes. You can also take another Snapshot on the same page or close this recording window.

As soon as you take a Snapshot, it will appear in your extension and app in a pending state. It can take up to a minute for a Snapshot to finish processing.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots#viewing-your-snapshots)

Viewing your Snapshots

Your Snapshots are created in your [Drafts](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/drafts-and-team-spaces)
 by default. You can always find all the Snapshots you have taken and the Team Snapshots you have access to in the web app at [app.plusdocs.com](https://app.plusdocs.com/)
.

You can also find the most recent Snapshots you've taken in your Plus extension. Click on them to open them in Plus.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FnHmDQgzxiNdVz3qP2x2d%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-23%2520at%252016.39.12%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b85c8db-608f-4d5f-902e-c566d7aa62c9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3bce9837&sv=2)

You can find all your Snapshots in the Plus web app

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots#refreshing-snapshots)

Refreshing Snapshots

By default, newly taken Snapshots will automatically refresh every day. You can update this setting in [Snapshot settings](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-settings)
.

You can also refresh a Snapshot at any time.

[PreviousUpdating the extension](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/chrome-extension/updating-the-extension)
[NextSites with smart capture](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/sites-with-smart-capture)

Last updated 25 days ago

# Create a Page | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/create-a-page#what-is-a-page)

What is a Page

A Page is where you can arrange multiple Snapshots and add context in a single view. It's a bit like a single slide where you can add Snapshots and text. The most common way people use Pages is to build mini "dashboards" with multiple Snapshots.

You can also [add Snapshots to Google slides](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace)
 and [embed them in other apps](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps)
, like Notion and Confluence.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fxb1wqmMaTHlLyBSyeOK3%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-22%2520at%252015.57.18%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De069056e-e122-4d54-ae28-5d3e7a0bf76d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c76b593&sv=2)

An example of multiple Snapshots on a Page in Plus

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/create-a-page#add-snapshots-to-a-page)

Add Snapshots to a Page

Open the Snapshot picker from the top of the Pages toolbar. From there, search for the Snapshot you want to use and click it to place it on the Page.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F2V8yvkPpMgDK9lmqnWn0%252FAdding%2520a%2520Snapshot%2520to%2520a%2520Page.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D830c7475-63ea-4691-80cb-d46bcf8cc25e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9edcfd7c&sv=2)

Adding a Snapshot to a Page

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/create-a-page#snapshots-refresh-automatically-and-on-demand)

Snapshots refresh automatically and on demand

Any Snapshots on a Page will update based on its "refresh rate" setting. Click on a Snapshot see its refresh setting or trigger a manual refresh.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FU68NJrWKAPUWIcu8kE17%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-22%2520at%252016.19.08%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7fea588-1a42-4703-aaf4-fba1e2110b46&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=31cb2c5d&sv=2)

Click on a Snapshot to change its refresh schedule or to manually refresh it

You can also refresh all the Snapshots on a Page at once when no Snapshot is selected.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FQkWxvQ9CcqVWgWl7uLHH%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-22%2520at%252016.15.58%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3111b599-a503-4edd-9114-a27d92bfb136&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f3c208d6&sv=2)

Refresh all the Snapshots on a Page at once

[PreviousTake a Snapshot](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/take-a-snapshot)
[NextShare with others](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/start-guide/share-with-others)

# Free and paid plans | Plus Guide

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/free-and-paid-plans#snapshot-limits)

Snapshot limits


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the free plan, there is a limit of 5 Snapshots per organization. You can upgrade to a paid plan to unlock 25 Snapshots. If you or your team needs more than 25 Snapshots, [contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/free-and-paid-plans#what-snapshots-count-toward-this-limit)

What Snapshots count toward this limit?

All Snapshots taken in your organization count toward this limit, including Snapshots in Personal and [Team](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/drafts-and-team-spaces)
 folders, as well as Snapshots set to manual refresh.

Deleted Snapshots do not count toward this limit.

There are no limits on the number of times you can use Snapshots on Pages or the number of Pages you can create.

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/free-and-paid-plans#what-happens-when-my-org-reaches-the-limit)

What happens when my org reaches the limit?

No one in the organization will be able to take new Snapshots.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/free-and-paid-plans#snapshot-refresh-rates)

Snapshot refresh rates


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the free plan, you can set Snapshots to automatically refresh every day or every 6 hours. You can upgrade to a paid plan to unlock hourly or 15 minute refresh rates.

Snapshots can always be manually refreshed as often as desired, by anyone in your org.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/free-and-paid-plans#upgrading-to-a-plan)

Upgrading to a plan


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Currently, only the owner of the organization can upgrade to a paid plan and manage an existing plan. If you're not the owner, contact them to make the upgrade.

The owner of the organization can pay to upgrade to a paid plan at any time from the Settings page in the Plus app.

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/free-and-paid-plans#how-do-i-upgrade-to-a-higher-tier)

How do I upgrade to a higher tier?

The organization owner can upgrade to a higher tier at any time from the Settings page in the Plus app. Click "Manage plan" to make the change.

You'll be immediately billed for the difference between the cost of the two plans, pro-rated based on how many days remain in your billing cycle.

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/free-and-paid-plans#is-there-a-discount-for-an-annual-plan)

**Is there a discount for an annual plan?**

Currently, only monthly billing plans are available.

**What if I need more than the paid plans offer?**

[Contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
 to tell us about what you need.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/free-and-paid-plans#downgrading-and-cancelling)

Downgrading and cancelling


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This also describes what happens if you previously had access to higher Snapshot limits as part of our beta program.

When your organization downgrades to a lower tier (or free) plan, you will no longer be able to take new Snapshots beyond the new plan limit. You will also not be able to set any Snapshots to the more frequent refresh rates.

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/free-and-paid-plans#how-do-i-cancel-a-paid-plan)

**How do I cancel a paid plan?**

The organization owner can cancel a paid plan at any time from the Settings page in the Plus app.

**What happens to my Snapshots beyond the limit?**

While you won't be able to take new Snapshots, existing Snapshots will remain in your organization.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/free-and-paid-plans#need-help)

Need help?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)

[PreviousShare links](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share/share-links)
[NextSnapshot integrations](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations)

# Ways to share | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share#id-1.-invite-someone-to-your-team)

1\. Invite someone to your Team

This is the best way to share content with your immediate team, coworkers, and other internal stakeholders. Team members have shared access to Snapshots and Pages in a Team space.

You can use the Team space to do things like create a shared folder of metrics you review weekly as a team, give visibility to your coworker who doesn't have access to the same tools you do, and allow an executive to quickly access important data from their phone.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share#id-2.-share-a-link-to-a-specific-piece-of-content)

2\. Share a link to a specific piece of content

If you only want to to share a specific piece of content with someone without allowing them to edit or refresh that Snapshot or Page, use a share link. This is a great way to share a specific set of information with a third party who shouldn't have access to the underlying app.

Share links can be private, public, or passcode protected. You can always update this setting later if you want to revoke access, for example.

[Share links](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share/share-links)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share#id-3.-use-an-integration-with-another-collaboration-tool)

3\. Use an integration with another collaboration tool

When you share Plus content using other tools, you can take advantage of the collaboration features and permissions/controls those other tools provide. For example, you can collaborate on a Google slides presentation or Notion document together with other teammates.

Learn more about the [Plus add-on for Google Slides and Docs](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace)
, [embedding Plus in other apps](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps)
, and [sharing Plus content in Slack](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack)
.

We're working on other integrations with communication and collaboration tools. If there is a specific one that is top-of-mind for you, [let us know](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

[Google Workspace](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace)
[Embed Plus in other apps](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps)
[App for Slack](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack)

[PreviousOrganizing your content](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/organizing-your-content)
[NextShare links](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share/share-links)

# Snapshot integrations | Plus Guide

You can embed Snapshots in other apps and automate your workflows in Google Slides, Google Docs, and Slack.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations#google-workspace)

Google Workspace

Stop copy/pasting screenshots in your Google Slides and Docs.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations#slack)

Slack

Send the latest metrics or data into Slack on a schedule.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations#notion)

Notion

Embed your live Snapshots directly in your Notion documents

# Connections | Plus Guide

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/connections#what-are-connections)

What are connections?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A connection represent Plus's ability to log into a site to take Snapshots. Each Snapshot belongs to a connection.

Currently, all the Snapshots you take on a site share a single connection. If you want to use two different accounts on the same site (e.g., a personal and work email), [let us know](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/connections#where-can-i-see-connections)

Where can I see connections?

You can see the status of each connection in the Snapshot viewer. You can also find the connections that need action in the [**Repair**](https://app.plusdocs.com/plus/snapshots/repair)
 section of the app.

Only the Snapshot owner can see (and repair) its connection.

![A screenshot of the Snapshot viewer highlighting the Connection in the sidebar](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fa8QTqWiFjyBNPJweTFgE%252FViewer_%2520Good%2520connection.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a78ae5b-2cc6-4fcf-a151-9059d5b002cc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c5fbd6ff&sv=2)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/connections#repairing-connections)

Repairing Connections


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/connections#why-do-i-need-to-reconnect)

Why do I need to reconnect?

Login sessions on sites expire routinely. When that happens, Plus also gets disconnected.

Log out frequency is determined by the site where you took the Snapshot and can vary. Some services, like banking apps, require you to log in after just a few minutes. These apps do not work well with Plus for that reason.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/connections#how-can-i-tell-when-i-need-to-reconnect)

How can I tell when I need to reconnect?

When we detect that a Snapshot connection needs repair, we will pause automatic refreshes of that Snapshot and send you an email.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F6EEul0ETC97rySu1xpZD%252FDisconnected.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ea521a4-f6ce-4f47-82cd-7b090c9d4443&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5df02a8d&sv=2)

You can also see any connections that need action in the [Repair section of the app](https://app.plusdocs.com/plus/snapshots/repair)
.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FuHuGwNafXVJVyxMPoM78%252FRepair.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8aeb1737-583b-4187-8e1f-8737fbd05482&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=be48dff1&sv=2)

Disconnected and deteriorating connections require repair

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/connections#how-do-i-repair-a-connection)

How do I repair a connection?

You can reconnect to a site from the Snapshot viewer or the connection page.

When you reconnect, Plus will refresh _all_ the Snapshots on that site that have been paused (and resume automatic refreshes.) You do not need to reconnect each Snapshot individually.

Only the Snapshot owner can repair its connection and see these options. You must have the Plus chrome extension installed to reconnect.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FDtogHp3uxI02X3Gaga2A%252FViewer_%2520Repair%2520connection.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0f0897e3-2318-4f0b-9029-97da1e7a1dfc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3bcdef36&sv=2)

Even if we didn't detect that a Snapshot connection is broken, you can always reconnect from the **Repair** menu.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FPN6NxaIXLD5KxtXi5Twx%252FCleanShot%25202023-03-21%2520at%252015.58.34%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f0faca2-18b2-4960-ba3b-590bc16a82c5&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c1e57ef5&sv=2)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/connections#troubleshooting-connections)

Troubleshooting connections


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
 if you need more help.

I can't seem to capture logged in Snapshots on this site/app.[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/connections#i-cant-seem-to-capture-logged-in-snapshots-on-this-site-app)

[Let us know](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
. There are [some sites](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/known-snapshot-issues)
 that we know don't work well with Plus, but we can always take a look and let you know if there's anything we can do.

This site is always getting disconnected.[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/connections#this-site-is-always-getting-disconnected)

Unfortunately, some apps and sites require you to log in very frequently (e.g., a banking app that signs you out after just a few minutes.) Plus will also get disconnected from these sites frequently and may not work well.

I use multiple logins on a site I want to Snapshot[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/connections#i-use-multiple-logins-on-a-site-i-want-to-snapshot)

Currently, all the Snapshots you take on a site share a single connection. If you want to use two different accounts on the same site (e.g., a personal and work email), [let us know](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

[PreviousSnapshot versions](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-versions)
[NextSnapshot repair](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-repair)

# Drafts and Team spaces | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/drafts-and-team-spaces#drafts)

Drafts

By default, Snapshots are saved to your Drafts, which are only visible to you.

Snapshots and Pages in your Drafts are only visible to you, unless you explicitly [share them via a public link](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share/share-links)
 or [embed them in another tool](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps)
, like Slack or Google slides.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FNCrxXYtFpIBFaPwcUAPL%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-23%2520at%252016.17.36%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c134c89-d12d-4f0d-8ec5-e3c6ff9fad7e&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=44ba91c2&sv=2)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/drafts-and-team-spaces#team-space)

Team space

The Team space is shared across and visible to everyone in your Organization. You can move Snapshots and Pages from your Drafts into the Team space. You can also create Pages directly in the Team space.

You can use the Team space to do things like create a shared folder of metrics you review weekly as a team, give visibility to your coworker who doesn't have access to the same tools you do, and allow an executive to quickly access important data from their phone.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/drafts-and-team-spaces#moving-content)

Moving content

You can move Snapshots and Pages between Drafts and your Team space by dragging and dropping from the grid or using the Move to action. You can also select multiple Snapshots to move them all at once.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F3SBg475g2mW3zIeXjOf3%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-23%2520at%252016.19.19.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2778bc76-f445-4b40-b269-f63690635300&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d49af106&sv=2)

Moving multiple Snapshots at once

[PreviousPage settings](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/pages/page-settings)
[NextOrganizing your content](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/organizing-your-content)

# App for Slack: FAQs | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack/app-for-slack-faqs#does-the-preview-image-update-automatically)

**Does the preview image update automatically?**

No, Slack does not allow us to automatically update the preview image. Plus will show you the latest version at the time the message was sent. In public channels, you can click on **Resend latest version** which will fetch the latest version of the Snapshot or Page and send a new message in the same channel. You can also set up a [recurring subscription](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack#slack-subscription)
 for Snapshots.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack/app-for-slack-faqs#what-types-of-plus-links-will-generate-previews)

**What types of Plus links will generate previews?**

The Plus app looks for URLs of Snapshots and Pages where the link sharing permission is set to "Anyone with the link can see this." If share link is not enabled, you will receive a message in Slack that prompts you to update the permission setting.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack/app-for-slack-faqs#who-sees-the-preview-images)

**Who sees the preview images?**

Anyone in your workspace will see the preview images, even if they don't have a Plus account. In order to access other options (like refreshing the Snapshot in Plus or creating a subscription), they will need to install the app and connect their Plus account.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack/app-for-slack-faqs#what-can-i-create-a-subscription-for)

What can I create a subscription for?

Currently, you can create subscriptions for Snapshots in public channels. If you'd like to create a subscription for a Page or set up a subscription in private channels or DMs, [let us know](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

[PreviousInstall the app for Slack](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack/install-the-app-for-slack)
[NextConnect to Notion](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/connect-to-notion)

# Snapshot tips and tricks | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-tips-and-tricks#what-can-i-snapshot)

What can I Snapshot?

You can Snapshot most websites and web apps from a computer browser.

You cannot Snapshot desktop apps or take Snapshots from your mobile device.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-tips-and-tricks#how-can-i-tell-if-something-will-snapshot-well)

How can I tell if something will Snapshot well?

If there is a distinct URL that consistently goes to the exact view you are trying to Snapshot, it will work well. An easy way to know what the Snapshot will capture is to refresh the page before taking a Snapshot. This view is what will get captured by the Snapshot.

This is especially useful when you have to apply filters to or otherwise customize a chart. For example, if the refresh preserved the the filters you applied, the chart will Snapshot well. If not, the Snapshot will only be able to capture the default view.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-tips-and-tricks#experimental-feature-replaying-clicks-and-other-actions)

🧪 Experimental feature: Replaying clicks and other actions

Sometimes the chart or view you want to capture can only be accessed after performing some actions (like clicking on a set of filters). In this case, [ask us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
 to enable "action recording," an experimental feature for you that will allow you to record these actions when taking a Snapshot.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FdkfheFMr735yxbFdhgvI%252FCleanShot%25202023-03-21%2520at%252014.29.22.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dde4711bf-9ad9-441c-aeb6-80388d770300&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=97f89785&sv=2)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-tips-and-tricks#scrolling-on-a-page)

Scrolling on a page

If you need to scroll down a page to capture something, Plus records your scroll position and replays it when refreshing the Snapshot. **However, you must use your mousewheel or trackpad to scroll.** Scrolling will not work if you are clicking and dragging a scrollbar.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-tips-and-tricks#changing-the-aspect-ratio-or-size-of-a-snapshot)

Changing the aspect ratio or size of a Snapshot

Adjusting the dimensions of your browser can help you get Snapshots in the right aspect ratio. For example, you can shrink the width of your browser to make a very wide chart narrower.

Example: Resizing the browser to get a narrower Snapshot

Similarly, you can also use your browser zoom to try to get the Snapshot you want. For example, you can zoom out to capture a larger portion of the page.

[PreviousSnapshot repair](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-repair)
[NextKnown Snapshot issues](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/known-snapshot-issues)

Last updated 2 years ago

# Page settings | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/pages/page-settings#page-settings)

Page settings

You can add a **Title** and **Description** to the Page to help you organize and search for content.

You can control [Snapshot Overlays](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-settings)
 for all the Snapshots on a Page at once. To set Snapshot Overlays for a specific Snapshot, just select one on the Page.

You can also manually **Refresh all Snapshots** on the Page at once.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/pages/page-settings#snapshot-specific-settings-on-a-page)

Snapshot-specific settings on a Page

To edit a specific Snapshot, select it on the Page. You will see additional options appear in the settings panel. You can control Snapshot Overlays, refresh the Snapshot, and edit Snapshot properties like the title and refresh rate. You can also initiate log back in for each Snapshot from here. [Learn more about Snapshot settings](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-settings)
.

Snapshot Overlay settings are specific to each Page, whereas Snapshot properties like title, description, and refresh rate will be reflected everywhere.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FMFEsM7Mz9pmou6zoYX0a%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-23%2520at%252016.03.04.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82356a06-93bd-4a23-9d8d-49395116bc1a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e74ef3c7&sv=2)

Select a Snapshot on a Page to update its refresh rate and other Snapshot-specific settings

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/pages/page-settings#snapshot-versions)

Snapshot versions

You can control whether a Page should automatically update a Snapshot as it refreshes ("most recent") or if you'd like to manually control which version is shown on the Page.

Manually controlling versions can be a good way to ensure you aren't surprised by what the viewers of the Page can see while still using Plus to automate pulling in new data when needed. You can also compare how data has changed over time by putting two different Snapshot versions side-by-side.

To set a Snapshot to automatically update as it refreshes, select the Snapshot on the Page. Then, click the "Most Recent" option on the version toolbar at the bottom of the Page.

To set a Snapshot to a specific version, select the Snapshot on the Page. Then, click the date and time option for the version you want in the version toolbar at the bottom of the Page.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FDPr397TvD3tImdHayAXE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4cc8c4ca-26b9-4490-ab44-c2986e6288f8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dc1b1ac0&sv=2)

Putting different versions of the same Snapshot on a Page

[PreviousPages](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/pages)
[NextDrafts and Team spaces](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/drafts-and-team-spaces)

# Known Google Slides and Docs issues | Plus Guide

If you have any questions about why something is not working or have feedback to help us prioritize, [let us know](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace/known-google-slides-and-docs-issues#multiple-google-accounts)

Multiple Google accounts

The Plus for Google Slides add-on does not support multiple Google accounts, so you should make sure you are only logged into the one you'd like to use with Plus. If you need, you can set up [Chrome profiles](https://support.google.com/chrome/answer/2364824)
 to manage multiple Google accounts more easily.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace/known-google-slides-and-docs-issues#repairing-snapshots)

Repairing Snapshots

Currently, when you click **Refresh Snapshots** in the sidebar, Plus will update the Snapshot image, even if that Snapshot cannot be refreshed because it is [logged out or needs review](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace/known-google-slides-and-docs-issues#repairing-snapshots)
.

To ensure you can always get the latest data in your slides and docs, make sure you open the Plus app and check for [any Snapshots that need repair](https://app.plusdocs.com/plus/snapshots/repair)
.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace/known-google-slides-and-docs-issues#editing-snapshots-in-google-slides)

Editing Snapshots in Google Slides

When you add a Snapshot to a Google Slide, it mostly behaves like an image. You can use the editing and styling tools in Google Slides on your Snapshots, but there are a few limitations.

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace/known-google-slides-and-docs-issues#editing-tools-that-work-with-refresh)

✅ Editing tools that work with refresh:

*   Resizing (without changing aspect ratio)
    
*   Move, rotate, copy and paste
    
*   Changing the order
    
*   Border styles (color, weight, dash), image effects (e.g., drop shadows)
    
*   Updating the hyperlink
    
*   Comments
    

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace/known-google-slides-and-docs-issues#editing-tools-that-do-not-work-when-you-refresh)

❌ Editing tools that do not work when you refresh:

*   **Crop** - When you refresh the Snapshot, the image will revert back to the entire Snapshot.
    
*   **Changing the aspect ratio** - When you refresh the Snapshot, the image will revert back.
    
*   **Grouping** - If you add a Snapshot to a group, you will not be able to refresh it.
    

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace/known-google-slides-and-docs-issues#editing-snapshots-in-google-docs)

Editing Snapshots in Google Docs

There are more limitations to how you can edit a Snapshot image in Google Docs.

✅ **Editing tools that work with refresh:**

*   Resizing (without changing aspect ratio)
    
*   Copy and paste
    
*   Updating the hyperlink
    

**❌ Editing tools that do not work when you refresh:**

*   Styling the image (borders, image effects)
    
*   Comments
    
*   Crop or resizing to change the aspect ratio of the image
    
*   Grouping
    

[PreviousGoogle Workspace](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace)
[NextApp for Slack](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack)

Last updated 2 years ago

Was this helpful?

# Organizing your content | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/organizing-your-content#folders)

Folders

You can create folders in your Drafts and Team space. You cannot nest folders, i.e., create a folder inside another folder.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FxblLR7i7NxOqw14G7ImT%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-23%2520at%252016.25.37%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1bbaf968-4025-4f34-9538-725e4b5b43ef&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8635c872&sv=2)

To move content into a folder, you can drag and drop from the grid or use the "Move to" action.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FN7LZBF4ppFDpgoNRmQFt%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-23%2520at%252016.26.55%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D834318b9-e931-4343-bcc2-dcc9f6ba5410&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9bb9f327&sv=2)

You can also select multiple items and move them at once.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FEBoQf87RA8yEermyGBTw%252Fmultiplesnapshotmove.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1923654f-bd28-42c3-8142-30a94717e213&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5fe79c74&sv=2)

Moving multiple Snapshots at once

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/organizing-your-content#search)

Search

You can search for Snapshots, Pages, and Folders across your Personal and Team spaces. You can search for:

*   Snapshot and Page titles and descriptions
    
*   Snapshot URLs
    
*   Text within Snapshots ✨
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FyqYIsHLuMHMxPNdLvwA0%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-23%2520at%252016.32.58.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D478a67e6-58d6-49fd-9cf1-f338eab81c88&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=19dd2619&sv=2)

Use search to find a specific piece of content

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/organizing-your-content#sort-and-filter)

Sort and filter

You can filter for Snapshots, Pages, and Folders and sort by Date created or the Name of the document.

# Pages | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/pages#what-is-a-page)

What is a Page

A Page is where you can arrange multiple Snapshots and add context in a single view. It's a bit like a single slide where you can add Snapshots and text. The most common way people use Pages is to build mini "dashboards" with multiple Snapshots.

You can also [add Snapshots to Google slides](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace)
 and [embed them in other apps](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps)
, like Notion and Confluence.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FwszJnl2o6duknbXspd32%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dffec3de8-bb2f-45fc-be78-032fe36f6f8b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4b3ed7dd&sv=2)

An example of multiple Snapshots on a Page in Plus

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/pages#add-snapshots-to-a-page)

Add Snapshots to a Page

Open the Snapshot picker from the top of the Pages toolbar. From there, search for the Snapshot you want to use and click it to place it on the Page.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FA6F9QspRo3A3I0s1cCgx%252FAdding%2520a%2520Snapshot%2520to%2520a%2520Page.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Decedd4cb-e9ab-4a83-abbb-9330f9004051&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=540def63&sv=2)

Adding a Snapshot to a Page

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/pages#snapshots-refresh-automatically-and-on-demand)

Snapshots refresh automatically and on demand

Any Snapshots on a Page will update based on its "refresh rate" setting. Click on a Snapshot see its refresh setting or trigger a manual refresh.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FHSswvibU7S3lXXk7cbJt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d0d257a-c4cb-4ec2-84dd-7e14ddf0cc72&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f175cb3a&sv=2)

Click on a Snapshot to change its refresh schedule or to manually refresh it

You can also refresh all the Snapshots on a Page at once when no Snapshot is selected.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FhSsAXBn9tbv2QBMUXcUt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcff5c8d3-b6fb-4adb-a5b1-66dcbaf03a4c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=39e8f23b&sv=2)

Refresh all the Snapshots on a Page at once

# Install the app for Slack | Plus Guide

Install our app for Slack to share Snapshots and Pages easily and set up scheduled automations for metrics, data, and other content.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack/install-the-app-for-slack#install-the-plus-app-for-slack)

Install the Plus app for Slack

From the [Plus app](https://app.plusdocs.com/)
, click on **Integrations** in the bottom left of the sidebar.

Then click on the "**Install app**" button under Slack. Make sure you are connected to the correct Slack workspace, then click "Allow." If your browser asks you, click on "Open this link in Slack."

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FvefVDIxR6uvDC3cQd3Mg%252FCleanShot%25202022-11-03%2520at%252016.07.53.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4017b112-09df-4b17-90d5-52968ae77f4e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8586bad3&sv=2)

Installing the app for Slack: Integrations > Install app

You should now be taken to the Plus app inside of Slack. Click on **Link my account**, which will open a Plus page in your browser. Click on **Link my account** to finish set up.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FbkZDaDaFzaqd7fgsWUAS%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-24%2520at%252011.40.57%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D11e846fe-e968-4cf1-b017-ac0f0dbbb9c9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6fb2e64f&sv=2)

Click "Link my account" to finish setting up the Plus app for Slack

# Known Snapshot issues | Plus Guide

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/known-snapshot-issues#limitations)

Limitations


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/known-snapshot-issues#unsupported-sites)

Unsupported sites

Some apps and sites are not compatible with how Plus captures Snapshots. If you want more information or would like to Snapshot these sites, [let us know](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

List of unsupported sites[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/known-snapshot-issues#list-of-unsupported-sites)

*   Patreon
    
*   Kickstarter
    
*   Zillow
    
*   Youtube Studio
    

**Sites that sometimes cannot be Snapshotted (depending on your settings)**

*   Meta / Facebook Business Suite
    

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/known-snapshot-issues#vpns)

VPNs

*   You cannot capture a Snapshot via a VPN connection.
    

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/known-snapshot-issues#frequent-logouts)

Frequent logouts

*   Sometimes you will need to reconnect Plus to the sites where you've taken Snapshots, just like how you have to periodically log back into the websites you use regularly.
    
*   For that reason, Plus does not work well on sites that ask you log back in very frequently, like most banking apps.
    
*   [Learn more about connections.](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/connections)
    

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/known-snapshot-issues#snapshot-accuracy-issues)

Snapshot accuracy issues


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sometimes, Plus Snapshots don't turn out exactly like you expected. These are some of the primary reasons you may get an inaccurate Snapshot.

To help us improve Plus, please let us know when your Snapshot doesn't look right. You can [contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
 or report an issue directly from the app.

![Report a Snapshot issue directly from the app. Click "Repair" and then "Report Snapshot issue"](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FLSbWvA01U1pCQbqgZ2ZN%252FCleanShot%25202023-01-26%2520at%252015.38.49%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db308bb10-09ed-468c-a106-78b6b1fb05ac&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2d2ac39a&sv=2)

Reporting a Snapshot issue from the app

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/known-snapshot-issues#scrolling)

Scrolling

*   Your scroll position won't be recorded properly in a Snapshot if you click and drag on a scrollbar. You should use your mousewheel or trackpad to scroll instead when you want to capture a Snapshot.
    

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/known-snapshot-issues#other-interactions)

Other interactions

*   If you have to add filters, select a specific tab, or click on an action like "run" or "generate chart" to get to a view you want, it may not Snapshot well.
    
*   If you can reload the page and get to the view you want, this means there is a unique URL that will Snapshot well. If you lose the settings you applied when you refresh the page, Plus will not be able to Snapshot what you need.
    
*   Examples of sites with this issue: Zendesk date filters, LinkedIn page analytics tabs.
    

🧪 **Experimental feature:** We are working on adding support for recording your actions, like clicking on a set of filters or a refresh button. [Contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
 to get early access.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/known-snapshot-issues#loading)

Loading

*   Occasionally, content that is slow to load won't Snapshot well, because the Snapshot service isn't always smart enough to know how long to wait for the page to load before capturing the Snapshot.
    
*   Examples: BI dashboards with lots of reports that load slowly.
    

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/known-snapshot-issues#a-d-blockers-and-other-extensions)

Ad blockers and other extensions

*   If you are using an ad blocker or are running another Chrome extension that changes the content on a site, Plus is not able to replicate those changes when taking a Snapshot, so you may notice that content is shifted in a Snapshot relative to what you see in your browser.
    
*   These problems can often be avoided by temporarily disabling your ad blocker (or other conflicting extensions), refreshing the page, and retaking the Snapshot.
    

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/known-snapshot-issues#location-time)

Location, time

*   If a website uses your current timezone or location, it may look different in a Snapshot.
    

[PreviousSnapshot tips and tricks](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-tips-and-tricks)
[NextPages](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/pages)

Last updated 2 years ago

Was this helpful?

# Snapshot FAQs | Plus Guide

What limits are there on the free plan?[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-faqs#what-limits-are-there-on-the-free-plan)

On the free plan, there is a maximum of 5 Snapshots per org, and a maximum refresh rate of 6 hours.

There are no limits on the number of Pages you can create, the number of times you can embed your Snapshots in other tools, or the number of teammates you can invite.

What if I need more Snapshots?[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-faqs#what-if-i-need-more-snapshots)

Upgrade to a paid plan to unlock more Snapshots and more frequent refresh rates. If your organization needs more than 25 Snapshots, [contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

How does Plus work?[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-faqs#how-does-plus-work)

Plus automates the process of visiting a website or app and taking a screenshot. Think of it as opening a new browser tab and taking a screenshot of the same area over and over again.

When you take a Snapshot, the Plus extension saves information about the state of your browser, like your cookies, local storage, session storage, the dimensions of your browser, and the bounding box of your Snapshot. With that information, we can automatically revisit that site or app as you and replicate the Snapshot you took.

Are there known limitations with Plus?[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-faqs#are-there-known-limitations-with-plus)

Snapshot capture does not work perfectly on all sites. Here are our [known Snapshot issues](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/known-snapshot-issues)
. If you run into others, please [contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

Why do my Snapshots get "logged out" from time to time?[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-faqs#why-do-my-snapshots-get-logged-out-from-time-to-time)

Since Plus essentially replicates the process where you open a browser tab and take a screenshot, we run into the same issues that you do.

We never store your username or password, so if your session expires on a website, we need you to log back in for Plus and refresh your session. [Learn more about connections.](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/connections)

Can I invite others to try Plus?[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-faqs#can-i-invite-others-to-try-plus)

Yes, please! Anyone can sign up, so feel free to tell others about Plus.

You can also invite team members who work with you to your organization to have shared access to Snapshots and Pages in a team space. Let us know if it would be helpful to set up a personalized onboarding for them.

How can I update the Plus extension?[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-faqs#how-can-i-update-the-plus-extension)

To update the Plus extension, [follow the steps in this support article](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/chrome-extension/updating-the-extension)
.

How can I provide feedback about Plus?[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-faqs#how-can-i-provide-feedback-about-plus)

[Contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
! We'd love to hear from you.

How does Plus handle security?[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-faqs#how-does-plus-handle-security)

We want to make it safe for you to use Plus across all your systems, and security is a priority for us. Today, we encrypt all sensitive data on your computer before it is sent to our servers, your data is encrypted in transit and at rest. Our employees do not have access to the private key to decrypt sensitive data.

Plus has attained SOC2 Type I compliance. You can request a copy of our report on our [security page](https://www.plusdocs.com/security)
.

Learn more about [security at Plus](https://www.plusdocs.com/security)
 or [contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

Can I delete my data?[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-faqs#can-i-delete-my-data)

Yes, send us an [email](https://guide.plusai.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#c9babcb9b9a6bbbd89b9a5bcbaada6aabae7aaa6a4)
, and we can permanently delete all of your data.

Is Plus down?[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-faqs#is-plus-down)

Check our [status page](https://status.plusdocs.com/)
 for information about service health and interruptions.

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-faqs#undefined)

[PreviousEmbed Plus in other apps](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps)

Last updated 25 days ago

You can refresh Snapshots, view previous versions, copy the Snapshot URL, and go to the source where the Snapshot was taken directly within Notion.

# Snapshot repair | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-repair#when-do-i-need-to-repair-a-snapshot)

When do I need to repair a Snapshot?

Occasionally, your Snapshots may need manual intervention in order to continue refreshing automatically.

The most common scenario is that you've been logged out of the website or app where you took your Snapshot. When that happens, you reconnect Plus, just as you would reauthenticate your account on that site.

[Connections](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/connections)

Your Snapshots may also need repair if something has changed on the page where you captured it. For example, someone reorganized a dashboard and now the chart you took a Snapshot of has moved or changed in dimensions. Or the app has been redesigned and your data has moved as a result.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-repair#paused-refreshes)

Paused refreshes

When Plus detects an issue with a Snapshot, we will pause automatic refreshes until you repair the Snapshot.

Broken versions are hidden when Snapshots viewed by others, including in embedded views, so your dashboards and reports don't look broken to viewers.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-repair#how-can-i-tell-when-i-need-to-repair-a-snapshot)

How can I tell when I need to repair a Snapshot?

Plus uses a machine learning model to detect issues and send you an email if a Snapshot might need repair.

You can find all of your Snapshots that might be broken in the Repair section of the web app.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FUuIv2GZenKIP6iuXSzAH%252FRepair.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e852ba4-9afc-4095-b7b3-6de30a98d70b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8a83f988&sv=2)

When you open a Snapshot that Plus has flagged as potentially broken, you'll see suggested instructions for fixing it.

Only the owner can see this message and repair the Snapshot.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FEkBt5uddVAXv4s4zen69%252FCleanShot%25202023-03-21%2520at%252019.41.25%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d5a1104-822e-40d7-bc78-c37f516dc357&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81d2fa03&sv=2)

A Snapshot that may be broken.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-repair#my-snapshot-looks-fine-even-though-plus-says-it-needs-review)

My Snapshot looks fine, even though Plus says it needs review

We use an AI to help us detect Snapshot issues. Sometimes the Plus AI will get it wrong and mark a good Snapshot as needing repair. If this happens, just let us know by clicking "**It looks normal.**" This will help the system improve over time.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FomiS2VkRVBpyvUGin3TQ%252FCleanShot%25202023-03-21%2520at%252019.45.36%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4663133e-ee21-4738-a892-3d4e1e09a9a9&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1484f469&sv=2)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-repair#how-to-repair-a-snapshot)

How to repair a Snapshot

Open the Snapshot in Plus. If we've detected an issue, we'll recommend a repair action, like "Reconnect" or "Take a new Snapshot."

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FSsTBBrT9ij6Mw2Ik7FDo%252FCleanShot%25202023-03-21%2520at%252019.55.00%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3231bb88-3161-4837-8e0b-e05936243d0a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=44d997d0&sv=2)

If we haven't detected an issue, you can always manually select an option from the **Repair** menu:

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FCvHBACId8E4R0Z3fsVWc%252FCleanShot%25202023-03-21%2520at%252019.51.05%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3bc8d5ab-b623-4e15-b10b-f17f489099b4&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=60440993&sv=2)

*   **Reconnect** if you've been logged out of the app or website.
    
*   **Retake Snapshot** if the content in the Snapshot has moved or changed.
    

When you repair a Snapshot, the Plus extension will open the source site or app in a new window (just like capturing a Snapshot), where you will be prompted to log back in and/or redo the capture process.

Snapshot repair requires the Plus Chrome extension. Only the Snapshot owner can repair it.

[PreviousConnections](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/connections)
[NextSnapshot tips and tricks](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-tips-and-tricks)

Last updated 2 years ago

Was this helpful?
