# Google Workspace | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace#what-is-the-google-workspace-add-on)

What is the Google Workspace add-on?

The Plus add-on allows you and your team to use your Snapshots in **Google Slides** and **Google Docs**. You can add Snapshots to your presentations and documents and refresh them in one click.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace#set-up)

Set up

Follow the link from the integrations menu in the app or go to the [Plus add-on in the Google Workspace Marketplace](https://workspace.google.com/marketplace/app/plus/214277172452)
 to install it.

The add-on does not support multiple Google accounts, so you should make sure you are only logged into the one you'd like to use with Plus. If you need, you can set up [Chrome profiles](https://support.google.com/chrome/answer/2364824)
 to manage multiple Google accounts more easily.

Open Plus from the **Extensions** menu in Google Slides or Google Docs. Sign in with your Plus account.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FsA1y8WEHTv0Xslp8ecxa%252FCleanShot%25202023-03-24%2520at%252011.19.01%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f53e352-245d-4e23-86be-85c61e84ebe4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b46a619&sv=2)

Open Plus from the Extensions menu in Google Slides and Google Docs

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace#adding-snapshots)

Adding Snapshots

Click on a Snapshot in the sidebar to add it to the current slide or position in your document. You can add any Snapshot that you have access to across both your Personal and Team spaces. You can also search and filter to more easily find the Snapshot you need.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FEfQ6vnDkWZg7lQwj7QQA%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-24%2520at%252011.14.57.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3f035c43-9e59-4e84-936e-4646b37218ea&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b48b71dd&sv=2)

Click on a Snapshot to add it to the Google Slide as an image

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace#snapshots-on-slides-and-in-docs)

Snapshots on slides and in docs

By default, Snapshots added to Google Slides (and Docs) have a link to the Snapshot in Plus. Open the Snapshot in the Plus app to access the source link, view more versions of the Snapshot, or repair the Snapshot.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F9la06a6ZqwshpkVybmD8%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-24%2520at%252011.33.48.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D51d6c59a-c5b9-4da7-8950-bb5e850e1262&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a3f40069&sv=2)

Opening a Snapshot on a Google Slide in Plus

This link is also a useful way to distinguish Snapshots from other images on your slides (and in your documents).

If needed, you can remove the link, just like editing any other image.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace#refreshing-snapshots)

Refreshing Snapshots

Once a Snapshot is added to a presentation (or document), **it will not automatically update** until you manually refresh it. So you will never be surprised by the contents of a presentation (or document).

When needed, you can refresh all the Snapshots in the presentation (or document) at once or refresh them individually from the sidebar.

When you click Refresh Snapshots:

*   ✅ Snapshots from your Personal space that you placed on the slide are refreshed
    
*   ✅ Snapshots from the Team space that anyone placed on the slide are refreshed
    
*   ❌ Snapshots that you do not have access to, like Snapshots in another person's Drafts, will **not** be refreshed.
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F1lZsJ5OEz53Nq4Vb52Zc%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-24%2520at%252011.25.16%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74c29c93-e46a-4f57-a2b7-a9cecd24c781&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ffc39c6e&sv=2)![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F3RSWEhmil5rY96NCFbab%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-24%2520at%252011.24.24%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0765b198-6e9c-4696-bc54-796cc4521395&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=802fd434&sv=2)

[PreviousSnapshot integrations](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations)
[NextKnown Google Slides and Docs issues](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace/known-google-slides-and-docs-issues)

# Share links | Plus Guide

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share/share-links#when-should-i-use-a-share-link)

When should I use a share link?

A share link is a great way to to quickly send a Snapshot or Page to someone, without giving them access to the underlying data or the whole library of content shared in the Team space. For example, you can send a marketing consultant a specific view of web traffic, without inviting them to your Team or giving them access to your analytics platform.

When collaborating with colleagues who should have access to a lot of the same content, we recommend inviting them to your Organization instead.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share/share-links#sharing-via-link)

Sharing via link

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FwnzR0yXwy2YA0XucSf38%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-23%2520at%252016.51.41%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e7d6b92-2103-4c63-9606-0f29ae58d8f8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2ccba3c7&sv=2)

You can share a link to a Snapshot, a Page, or a specific Snapshot version from the share menu in the web app.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share/share-links#permissions)

Permissions

By default, Snapshots and Pages are set to "Anyone with the link can see this." This allows you to easily and conveniently share your content or embed it in other tools.

Your content will only be visible if you've explicitly decided to share it. It is nearly impossible to guess the URLs of your Snapshots and Pages, and your content is not accessible via search engines.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F9gvCQAz1ohtQ36u2zmNc%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-24%2520at%252010.08.45%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db879f890-f012-4be7-9bd5-90ab3f2d8196&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8badfbf3&sv=2)![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FZlKt3vjkOpcBCGLwSoqz%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-24%2520at%252010.08.54%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D004c799f-ac82-4d4e-8b6e-6aaeef5769b1&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58f7c69b&sv=2)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share/share-links#sharing-a-specific-snapshot-version)

Sharing a specific Snapshot version

You can share a specific version of a Snapshot by selecting in the Snapshot viewer, clicking share, and then checking the option to "Share only this version." This can be useful for pointing the viewer to a specific point-in-time, like highlighting something that happened last week.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FjVYhcEkh8YlDBYHkFHhr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3c990aec-933a-4978-9db8-a57209f370c5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b2352e08&sv=2)

Sharing a specific version of a Snapshot

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share/share-links#what-does-the-viewer-see)

What does the viewer see?

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FYCj258MROMDwNpRgkX2c%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-24%2520at%252010.11.01%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8f92d4d2-7e2e-4d60-b2ad-172d0387e6ae&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bac0ef48&sv=2)

Example of a view-only link to a Snapshot

Anyone not logged into a Plus account will only see the Snapshot or Page you shared. They will not be able to view or update settings, refresh Snapshots, see the refresh schedule or the URL of the datasource, or access any of your other Snapshots or Pages.

This also applies to content you've [embedded in other apps](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps)
.

**Pro-tip:** You can use Snapshot overlays to add metadata and context when sharing via link. Learn more: [Snapshot settings](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshots/snapshot-settings)
.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share/share-links#revoking-access)

Revoking access

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F31JpeDpqteFbx1xs8Jct%252FCleanShot%25202022-08-24%2520at%252010.12.44%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0ebf1ac3-aa3b-403f-9767-1824b6e941b0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=27f71a0e&sv=2)

If you share a link with someone then change the setting back to "Only I can see this," public access will be revoked via both the share URL and embeds in other tools.

[PreviousWays to share](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share)
[NextFree and paid plans](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/free-and-paid-plans)

Last updated 2 years ago

# App for Slack | Plus Guide

Use the Plus app for Slack to share Plus content with your team.

You can share Snapshots with others in your Slack workspace, even if they're not logged into Plus (or your BI tool or CRM or other dashboards where the Snapshot was taken.)

You can also set up a recurring subscription in Slack to automatically send a Snapshot on a schedule you choose, like "Send this MRR metric to the #gtm channel every day at 9AM."

[Install the app for Slack](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack/install-the-app-for-slack)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack#sharing-plus-content-in-slack)

Sharing Plus content in Slack

When you send a Plus URL in a Slack message, the Plus app will unfurl a preview of that Snapshot or Page.

Note: This preview is a static image that does not automatically update.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fjgm2jusoMA1IjbJ3qwAm%252FCleanShot%25202022-11-03%2520at%252016.17.51%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df4ba7c55-cfba-4517-b1a2-a439300a528b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=262af470&sv=2)

Plus Snapshots in Slack

In public channels, if you have access to the Snapshot, you can click on the **More options** button to open it in Plus, send the latest version to the channel, or set up a recurring subscription.

You have access to the Snapshot if you're the owner or the Snapshot is in your [Team space](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/drafts-and-team-spaces)
 AND you've [linked your Plus account to Slack](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack/install-the-app-for-slack)
.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FQUm5WSsBCvm55VTE34Ye%252FCleanShot%25202022-11-03%2520at%252016.20.48%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da91fa29b-9c6b-437c-b034-e69d0e5d2879&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=921f9394&sv=2)

More options include sending the latest version or creating a subscription

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack#slack-subscription)

Set up a subscription

Subscriptions are only available for Snapshots in public channels currently. [Let us know](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
 if you need subscriptions for Pages or private channels and DMs.

Subscriptions allow you specify a recurring schedule on which a Snapshot will be sent to a public channel automatically, like "Send this MRR Snapshot to `#gtm-updates` every Monday at 9AM."

Create a new subscription from the **More options** popup above or from Plus app home tab in Slack.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FtwMjcamx6kFaa96nJNWl%252FCleanShot%25202022-11-03%2520at%252016.29.00%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc70d8a91-40c1-4d52-9dcd-d782e128f018&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=540069d7&sv=2)

Create a new subscription from the Plus app home tab in Slack.

Specify a Plus URL (if you're starting from scratch), pick a destination channel, select which days you want the message to send, and specify a time.

You can also schedule a refresh 5 minutes before the subscription time, to ensure that the Snapshot will have the latest data when it sends.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FrbHsEEcvl8WoL9jb6t4p%252FCleanShot%25202022-11-03%2520at%252016.39.00%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1e01003e-b90c-4dd8-8330-bcc5ec34916a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e57283d1&sv=2)

Creating a new subscription in Slack

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack#manage-subscriptions)

Manage subscriptions

A list of your subscriptions can be found on the home tab of the Plus app in Slack. You can also delete subscriptions from here.

Only the creator of the subscription can delete it.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fpno1a6Q4YJPaz25re6rR%252FCleanShot%25202022-11-03%2520at%252016.51.18%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c9a7dc5-813d-42c5-ba37-b0bf968fc4a6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5f704225&sv=2)

View and delete your existing subscriptions in the Home tab of the Plus app in Slack.

[PreviousKnown Google Slides and Docs issues](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace/known-google-slides-and-docs-issues)
[NextInstall the app for Slack](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/app-for-slack/install-the-app-for-slack)

# Embed Plus in other apps | Plus Guide

You can embed Plus Snapshots and Pages in your existing document editors and other productivity tools, so you can replace static screenshots in your weekly meeting docs with Snapshots that automatically update.

Use a different productivity tool that's not listed here? [Let us know](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps#how-embeds-work)

How embeds work

Example of a real Snapshot embedded on this page

Embedded Snapshots and Pages stay up-to-date. Viewers can navigate to other versions of the Snapshot and open the Snapshot in Plus. Logged in viewers with access to the Snapshot can also refresh it or go to the source link.

[Share permissions](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/ways-to-share/share-links)
 will apply to embedded content as well, so make sure the Snapshot or Page is in the Team space (only your teammates who are logged into Plus will be able to see it) or set it to "Anyone with the link can see this."

To embed a specific version of a Snapshot, use the link for a specific version. If you embed a specific version, it will not automatically update as the Snapshot refreshes, but you'll still be able to open the original Snapshot.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FwtlBK7MLO6LinfMkT8W5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0788db1a-1717-4cc7-8271-68a34a75e7c0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3dcbc7ab&sv=2)

Sharing a specific version of a Snapshot

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FgYmpVRzVxHNY1X3ph9Ok%252FCleanShot%25202022-10-31%2520at%252016.05.06.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6d7cfc28-fdb1-440b-b626-53c1a8f7239d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c063096&sv=2)

Example of embedding a Snapshot in Notion

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps#document-editors)

Document editors

Notion[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps#notion)

Add Plus to Notion [here](https://www.notion.so/integrations/plus-8f25d2b0-81cf-46f9-a2ac-1bea17d57f19)
.

Copy the URL you want to embed. Paste it directly into Notion. If you haven't already connected Plus, follow the instructions to do so.

Select **Paste as Preview.**

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FU1bVjrgD73WvkF6HQtbF%252FCleanShot%25202023-02-24%2520at%252015.16.57%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9e794ad-f1c3-44fd-8d99-37298e31d632&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2721df56&sv=2)

Learn more about [connecting Plus to Notion](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/connect-to-notion)
.

Coda[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps#coda)

**Embed in your content**

Copy and paste the URL you want to embed. On paste, select the "Embed" option. As a shortcut, you can use the `/embed` command.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FQVNtU6zW7znn3Fnovrv8%252FCleanShot%25202022-06-22%2520at%252013.12.38%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D78ca8a46-6124-442b-948d-4a9658ccc235&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9e8469fc&sv=2)

**Embed as a page**

Either select “New embed” from the “New page” dropdown below your list of pages in the left sidebar, or click the 3 dot menu on an existing page in the sidebar and select “Add embed.” As a shortcut, you can use the `/page` embed command.

![image.png](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcodahosted.io%2Fdocs%2FAR0uNTULD9%2Fblobs%2Fbl-zGJq2YCn0P%2F9a7366ccd926c993db36aff66f54791687bbe230f630753294684fbd2b1d9d0f22e1f396c1208aa3eba6a763c87edcfe340004e40615f34de48dbcb7f348e7c2b19c77a9cc4f70b2fa5f8c9a264a1b765203a31db6ece27ef74a6905341f6ae9866b4c94&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebd3bbe7&sv=2)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FDTlqwPa9O7IKiov7Z9If%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc827e582-e83a-4fdf-8fd5-876122d84acc&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6d902a37&sv=2)

**Alternatively,** add the [Plus Coda Pack](https://coda.io/packs/plus-17261)
 to your doc.

Use the Plus formula `=Snapshot('URL')` and `=Page('URL')` to embed your Snapshot or Page. Make sure you include the URL in quotes.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FtC3vTOGC50LlGKr48O5j%252Fcodapack.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc9a1175-b287-4606-9681-e9e503c93e7f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ec68fb1b&sv=2)

Learn more about [embedding apps like Plus into Coda](https://help.coda.io/en/articles/1211364-embedding-content-in-your-doc)
.

Slite[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps#slite)

Copy and paste the URL you want to embed. It will automatically unfurl.

Confluence[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps#confluence)

Paste a Plus URL into your document. Click on the link badge and select "Embed" from the menu.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FyZ1RVKdPnIojASEzSHGb%252FCleanShot%25202023-01-13%2520at%252010.06.16%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D25f95226-85d4-4155-be35-574613619149&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d825ae8&sv=2)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fjh2bpxhL83ngYRSE8SBq%252Fconfluence-embed.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a240bfd-bfb3-4a77-83e1-613dba36be29&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a61417b5&sv=2)

Obsidian[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps#obsidian)

Use an [iframe](https://help.obsidian.md/Editing+and+formatting/Embedding+web+pages)
 to embed Plus Snapshots and Pages in [Obsidian](https://obsidian.md/)
.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps#presentations-and-canvases)

Presentations and canvases

Google Slides[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps#google-slides)

Use our [Google Slides add-on](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/google-workspace)
.

Canva[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps#canva)

Click **⋯ More** from the editor side panel and select **Embeds**. Paste in the Plus URL you want to embed.

💡 **Beware:** There is a Canva bug where some embeds don't display properly when you first add them. Refresh the page and it should work.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F1NVlkAKXh6mFMyuXkF3t%252FCleanShot%25202022-06-22%2520at%252013.25.27%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfcce1f8b-106e-4cb8-a301-ab62d664e279&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=30528122&sv=2)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FzW97JgpwptgvWbWRbVAl%252FCleanShot%25202022-06-22%2520at%252013.26.07%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D85bda580-a72f-4987-80fc-11de8d89e679&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8c4675f&sv=2)

Plus actions (go to source, share, refresh) are only available in presentation mode.

Read more: [https://www.canva.com/help/embed-media/](https://www.canva.com/help/embed-media/)

Gamma[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps#gamma)

Embed Plus in [Gamma](https://gamma.app/)
 presentations. Use `/embed` and select **Webpage or app**. Paste in the URL of the Plus Snapshot you want to embed. Then open the dropdown and select **Inline** instead of Preview.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FGK8XZN9abrAwR8V3wbvZ%252FCleanShot%25202022-12-19%2520at%252013.45.12%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D35077096-e1c6-4aca-a767-050d578bde57&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b1e70807&sv=2)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FlAGYWfh3y7rymJOvVtjB%252FCleanShot%25202022-12-19%2520at%252013.48.03%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb360331-9572-4212-865c-1108e8418c64&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e070b51b&sv=2)

Tome[](https://guide.plusai.com/other/live-snapshots/snapshot-integrations/embed-plus-in-other-apps#tome)

You can embed Plus Snapshots in [Tome](https://beta.tome.app/)
. See an example [here](https://tome.app/plus/startup-funding-landscape-cl9nex45a10038914v8h2zlfooc8)
.

Click the + sign and then URL to **add a new tile**. Paste in a Plus URL you want to embed.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FvpUAFqGHUWczfOmRVGts%252FCleanShot%25202022-12-19%2520at%252013.34.20%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7174622c-283a-4aa6-b64c-674ca640fe63&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=323ff12b&sv=2)

 blocks. Type `/embed` to create an embed block. Paste in the Plus URL you want to embed.

# Custom templates (beta) | Plus Guide

This is a **beta** feature and may be buggy.

Custom templates are only available in **Google Slides** for now and require a **Team** plan.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#what-are-custom-templates)

What are custom templates?

When you import a custom template, we convert it into a format that can be used by Plus AI — including when [generating a presentation](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation)
, [inserting](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide)
 a single slide, and [remixing](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/remix-slides)
 slides.

We will use the slides in your template **as-is** — Plus AI will not redesign your slides or add new slide types.

This article will walk you through how to prepare your template before importing.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#requirements)

Requirements

**Google Slides only**

*   Your template must be a Google Slides presentation in your Google Drive
    
*   You must log into Plus with the Google account that has access to that Google Drive file
    
*   PowerPoint support is coming soon
    

**Supported slides** — These elements can be updated by AI

*   Text-only slides
    
*   Text and image slides
    

**Unsupported elements** — These will be imported as static elements and cannot be updated by AI

*   [See below](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#slides-to-avoid)
    
*   If you need to use these types of slides with AI, [contact us](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
     about Enterprise solutions.
    

**Limits**

*   Each template has a maximum of 25 slides, including title, agenda, and dividers
    
*   You can import up to 5 custom templates
    

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#preparing-a-template-for-import)

Preparing a template for import


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#sample-template)

Sample template

[https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/1msBcDg5AIWG4q8k7PORFniDy\_D0Shoe85d5q6QYZZ6Y/](https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/1msBcDg5AIWG4q8k7PORFniDy_D0Shoe85d5q6QYZZ6Y/)

To edit this file, save a copy to your own Google Drive first! **File > Make a copy > Entire Presentation**

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#template-prep-checklist)

Template prep checklist

1

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#set-up-your-template)

Set up your template

*   Your template must be a Google Slides file in your **Google Drive**.
    
*   If you're adapting our example template or an official company template, make a copy first.
    
*   Give it a unique name that you can easily find later, like "Template - Copy for PlusAI".
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FFRN6WdtlKI6YCdsCBZSf%252FCustom%2520template%2520-%2520make%2520a%2520copy%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43874c33-926e-45bb-9564-326ee778fe1c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=259742ff&sv=2)

*   Launch the slide master / theme builder ( **View > Theme builder** )
    
*   Update theme colors and fonts, if needed
    
    ![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FvpOyujOzVzdI4ekxNlCa%252FCleanShot%25202025-06-11%2520at%252013.54.29%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8ad2b167-1c47-454d-92fd-299b9f00c53a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e6c480e7&sv=2)
    

2

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#move-footers-and-logos-into-the-slide-master-theme-builder)

Move footers and logos into the slide master / "theme builder"

*   Move any repeating, static text — disclaimer, copyright, company name — into the theme builder slides. Otherwise, AI will rewrite this text!
    
*   Copy and paste static elements into the slide master. Remember to delete any duplicate elements left on the slide. You should not be able to click on or select these elements in the normal editing view.
    
*   For best results, do the same with any logos that repeat on every slide.
    

3

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#select-the-slides-you-want-to-import)

Select the slides you want to import

*   Maximum of 25 slides, including titles, agendas, dividers
    
*   Make sure there is exactly one copy of each template slide
    
    *   ⚠️ Layouts that are in the slide master but NOT the actual file will not be imported
        
    
    ![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FH9LILoxdTdTvE1t53XZg%252Fcustom%2520template%2520-%2520hidden%2520layouts%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D95570a29-a298-4653-b760-b0a0ad3ed81a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=57b5a9f7&sv=2)
    
    *   Delete any duplicate slides you don't want to import twice
        
    
*   Remove extraneous slides that are not part of the template itself
    
    *   instructions
        
    *   brand guidelines
        
    
*   Remove [slides that won't work well](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#slides-to-avoid)
    , including
    
    *   tables, charts, diagrams
        
    *   assets that come from a specific library (e.g., custom icons)
        
    
*   Remove static slides that are not meant to be updated — you can copy/paste these into the presentation afterward
    
    *   thank you slide, legal disclaimers
        
    *   mission statement, pricing chart, team page
        
    *   ⚠️ **If you import these, AI will rewrite them!**
        
    

4

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#optimize-text-elements)

Optimize text elements

*   Don't use inline formatting within the same text element — Each distinctly formatted piece of text should be in its own text box.
    
    *   For example, a header should be in a separate text box from the supporting content.
        
    
    ![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FWHz89Ipe9BCNQhWtljy6%252Fcustom%2520template-%2520text%2520%283%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6a419ec-6b4e-4e7e-8b91-1841abe1ba4d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d5a0918d&sv=2)
    
*   For best results, use **sample text** instead of empty placeholders — the more specific the better, for example
    
    *   length — fill in the entire text box, don't leave it at 1 example bullet
        
    *   content — If it's a generic slide, lorem ipsum is fine, but if it's a case study, write an actual example.
        
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FDioQN2OosuXdfv9XiIxS%252Fcustom%2520template-%2520placeholder.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab68354e-972e-4ec9-b01d-4dfaf934f5d3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7aa7ea5e&sv=2)

5

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#optimize-images)

Optimize images

*   Our AI importer will do its best to distinguish the content-related images — which will be updated with relevant AI-generated imagery when you use your template — from decorative elements.
    
*   We recommend moving decorative images (including background images) into the slide master.
    
*   Alternatively, add the image as the slide background (**Background** button in the toolbar) — just make sure you can't click to select the background image on the slide.
    
    ![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FfrsqwkT5x6qoryxblkrT%252FCleanShot%25202025-06-13%2520at%252012.00.18%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db0b140f8-d018-4e72-839b-0f5abd16cb60&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea9818ba&sv=2)
    
    With no elements selected, use the "background" button in the toolbar to set a background image
    
*   For best results, avoid overlapping images.
    
*   You can add up to 10 images per slide.
    

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#slides-to-avoid)

Slides to avoid

These slides won't work well with Plus AI and we recommend removing them from your template before importing.

Support for all of these slides are available on PlusAI Enterprise — [send us your template to get a quote](https://guide.plusai.com/help/contact-us)
.

Charts[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#charts)

*   We don't support native charts and graphs with custom templates yet — even though you can generate charts with our [public templates](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/templates)
    .
    
*   If you import a slide with a chart, PlusAI can fill in the text elements, but the chart will not be updated.
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Ffvtx2Dt97mOvLNGbvgNv%252FCleanShot%25202025-06-05%2520at%252010.38.45%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf9c13cc-a178-43f9-93cf-9db6f7fa801d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f679cc8a&sv=2)

Example chart slide — ❌ AI can update the slide text, but won't be able to update the chart

Tables (native element)[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#tables-native-element)

*   Tables are not yet supported by PlusAI
    
*   If your table always has the same number of rows and columns, convert it into individual text boxes before importing the template
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FKoXAzOizo1rMXFzvfKOt%252FCleanShot%25202025-06-05%2520at%252010.50.46.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da7fc4b6c-6dbf-45a4-a8b7-364d12598787&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=198704e8&sv=2)

Example of a "table" made with individual text boxes — ✅ works with PlusAI

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FDBPcMhYgUjFVHH4FoGpX%252FCleanShot%25202025-06-05%2520at%252010.51.52%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df87433e0-2cda-4928-a45b-f06458104eb6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81010d4f&sv=2)

Example of a native table in Google Slides — ❌ not compatible with PlusAI

Diagrams, gantt charts, comparison matrices[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#diagrams-gantt-charts-comparison-matrices)

*   Currently, you can use custom templates to generate basic text and image slides — PlusAI does not understand how to fill out a complicated diagram.
    
*   _Examples: Gantt charts, matrices with repeating symbols_
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FBKZlKp07AsiwrD8lmwsD%252FProject%2520Timeline%2520Presentation%2520%28Google%2520Template%29%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dce4050fb-4a5c-4e9e-a1e4-aff46a05ada4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d3d156c&sv=2)

Example matrix — ❌ AI can fill out the text elements, but can't swap out the RACI icons

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FHl0ZK6BeKgvEc9r9r9ce%252FProject%2520Timeline%2520Presentation%2520%28Google%2520Template%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5447d383-6778-4947-b38f-f9888ad99dbf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=87a1968c&sv=2)

Example Gantt — ❌ AI can fill out tasks and dates, but can't update the bars or add/remove rows

Static / library slides that are not meant to be rewritten[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#static-library-slides-that-are-not-meant-to-be-rewritten)

*   If you import these slides, PlusAI will overwrite the text when generating your slides
    
*   We recommend copy/pasting these into your deck after generating with AI, or using [insert](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide)
     to add individual slides to customize your existing presentation.
    
*   _Examples: Mission statement, About us, Feature comparisons, Thank you_
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FbE1KDp7neYwDMJyJidd9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd3562e36-d0da-4405-aee9-c4b0ba881ffc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17499668&sv=2)

Example team slide from HomeCooks pitch deck — ❌ remove before import

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FkC2vnAo0wFOwbSSMQ16b%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D79e032a3-8e89-4748-800f-96aa81cfbc97&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=77b75fbc&sv=2)

Example mission statement from Smalls pitch deck — ❌ remove before import

Instructions, brand guidelines, icon/image libraries[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#instructions-brand-guidelines-icon-image-libraries)

*   Remember to remove any slides that are not part of the template before importing
    
*   _Examples: Instructions, brand guidelines, sample icon/images_
    

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F5Okb86buFvlS3dF2WHQO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D719607a2-9beb-4fc8-aad2-32a7d4a94a70&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=16e66613&sv=2)

Example of a Brand Guideline slide from Zapier — ❌ remove before import

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FOjDT9tSmcZeCtWRnnPln%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ba8aa49-3feb-4c6f-bcd2-46ba70f149a8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d086155d&sv=2)

Example of a sample icon slide from Zapier — ❌ remove before import

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#import-a-custom-template)

Import a custom template


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After preparing your template, you're ready to import it into Plus.

Launch **Plus AI > New Presentation**. Then click on **Custom templates**.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FE9haGrO70Kr8Te1dqwPy%252FCleanShot%25202025-06-05%2520at%252011.12.29%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2dca8b73-ed54-4700-ac14-2a88f290e1eb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2d1c76dd&sv=2)

Import a custom template: Launch Plus AI > New Presentation > Custom templates

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#importing)

Importing

1.  **Name** your template. Remember that your template will be visible to everyone on your team
    
2.  If you'd like, add a **description** to give your teammates more context — e.g., "Only use this for internal meetings". This is visible when someone clicks on the template preview
    
3.  Select your template file in Google Drive
    
4.  Click **import**
    
5.  Wait your template to process — This can take a minute or two. In the meantime, you can use other PlusAI features or close the add-on.
    

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#how-it-works)

How it works

When you import a template, we automatically make a copy of your presentation before converting it into a format that is usable by PlusAI.

Therefore, any changes you make to your original template later will NOT be reflected in Plus. This also means you can safely delete and move your original file without affecting your new custom template.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#managing-custom-templates)

Managing custom templates


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Custom templates are shared across your team. Each team can have a maximum of 5 custom templates.

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#editing-your-templates)

Editing your templates

Currently, you cannot edit a template once it's been imported. Delete the template and reimport it to make changes.

#### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#deleting-your-template)

Deleting your template

Click on the 3-dot (**...**) menu to delete a custom template.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-templates-beta#using-custom-templates)

Using custom templates


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use custom templates when [generating a presentation](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation)
, [inserting](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide)
 a single slide, and [remixing](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/remix-slides)
 slides.

[PreviousTemplates](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/templates)
[NextCustom branding](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/custom-branding)

Last updated 26 days ago

# Plus AI changelog | Plus Guide

Feature: Plus AI for PowerPoint

[Plus AI for PowerPoint](https://guide.plusai.com/plus-ai/install-in-powerpoint)
 is finally here.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FkYZNq5dDE2Pso0mOtBUP%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-25%2520at%252017.39.30%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd3928108-f5ee-4ac0-bca1-6623a881e221&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8541f8d8&sv=2)

Improvements and bug fixes

*   Improved and expanded template designs
    
*   Improved quality of AI generated content for certain types for slides
    
*   Fixed a bug where the number of slides setting wasn't working properly

May 2024


--------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#enhancement-auto-presentation-length)

Enhancement: Auto presentation length

We added an "Auto" option when generating a presentation, so you can let the AI decide how long the presentation should be.

You can still specify the exact presentation length you want via settings when generating a presentation.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#improvements-and-bug-fixes-1)

Improvements and bug fixes

*   Fixed an issue where the Plus AI add-on didn't load
    
*   Improved and expanded template designs
    
*   Improved quality of AI generated content for certain types for slides
    

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#april-2024)

April 2024

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#feature-design-update)

We revamped the design of the Plus AI for Google Slides add-on to make it easier to use and work better with our custom templates.

We also improved the discoverability and usability of different modes for generating presentations

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#improvements-and-bug-fixes-2)

Improvements and bug fixes

*   Improved error handling when slide generation fails during presentation generation

*   Fixed presentation template issues and improved design.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FWhYFxDSZxPRI2sKhtoU9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87798182-d16b-4a63-85ec-24f3244fa51c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d36d8763&sv=2)

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#enhancement-preserve-text-mode)

Enhancement: Preserve text mode

Now you can choose whether you want the AI to **preserve or enhance** your source text when generation a presentation from a [document](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file)
 (or pasting in text). [Learn more.](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file#enhance-vs-preserve)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FOivneIo1dfrLdm2v8Dbi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2933642b-6b4d-485a-aa24-561f79d5ff44&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=741376b1&sv=2)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#new-feature-plus-ai-for-google-docs)

New feature: Plus AI for Google Docs

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252F77UowOq4SkhjDspvRZj8%252Funnamed%2520%282%29.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D165c82b2-4db6-44eb-9485-95c8a3f6e036&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=738f3086&sv=2)

Using Plus AI in Google Docs to rewrite a document

You can now generate, rewrite, and translate text directly in Google Docs using the same Plus AI for Google Workspace add-on. Google Docs functionality is included in all Plus AI subscriptions. [Learn more.](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-google-docs/generate-a-new-document)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#new-feature-document-to-presentation)

New feature: Document to presentation

Instead of copying and pasting, you can now upload a PDF or other text document directly to [generate a presentation](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file)
.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FPGE50XzxRDKZgKit4pjt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De283e548-d70f-4e4a-93e6-e9ba965ceb98&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3289546a&sv=2)

You can upload a file to transform it into a presentation

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#enhancement-rewrite-all-slides)

Enhancement: Rewrite all slides

We added a button so you can [rewrite](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/rewrite-slides)
 — and [translate](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/languages)
 — all the slides in a presentation in one click.

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FiGeCfGsuleNWO6IpPnPc%252Funnamed.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De514f3c4-9898-4d3c-b33a-7e5b09def17c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4fafc38a&sv=2)

New option to rewrite all the slides in your presentation at once.

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#improvements-and-bug-fixes-4)

Improvements and bug fixes

*   Improved loading experience in Insert, Remix, and Rewrite, so you can see your progress and you're less likely to interrupt an existing request.
    
*   Improved interface when selecting a paid subscription.
    
*   Faster and more accurate icon selection when generating slides.
    
*   Fixed a bug where language settings weren't correctly applied in Slide by slide and Text to presentation modes.
    
*   Fixed a bug in Slide by slide mode where slide titles were not accurately followed.
    
*   Fixed a bug in Document upload where the contents were not correctly passed along to the AI model to generate content.

We also added a language dropdown to make it easier to generate non-English output.

We now ask you for feedback every time you generate a new presentation or slide. This qualitative feedback directly helps us improve Plus AI.

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#improvements-and-bug-fixes-5)

Improvements and bug fixes

*   Improved presentation generation quality and speed, including reducing instances where slides have empty or placeholder content.
    
*   Improved reliability and quality of images on slides. Fixed a bug where slides were only using placeholder images.
    
*   Added more detailed and helpful error messaging when Plus AI fails.
    
*   Fixed a bug where presentations that did not generate successfully still counted against free plan usage limits.
    
*   Fixed a bug where sometimes users could not be removed from an organization.
    
*   Updated the Google Slides add-on to prevent you from submitting empty prompt. (It doesn't produce a good result 😅)
    
*   Fixed a bug where some empty slides were available in the Insert and Slide by Slide layout selector.

Feature: Presentation presets

[Presets](https://guide.plusdocs.com/plus-ai/team-library/prompt-presets)
 allow you and your team to save frequently used prompts and settings to your team library, to save you time when generating recurring presentations, like client proposals or quarterly business reviews. [Learn more.](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets/prompt-presets)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FX31qQt1UunXjZptEnUjW%252F2023-11-06%2520preset.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddcdebc9e-5f70-4fc9-9ca9-644105d9d766&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7b3b2779&sv=2)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#feature-prompt-history)

Feature: Prompt history

We added [history](https://guide.plusdocs.com/plus-ai/history)
 to help you generated you’ve generated (since 10/15/2023). You can open the original Google Slides document where the slides were generated, rerun the prompt, or save it as a preset. [Learn more.](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/history)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FOEUEBRs8ntsWfYq3yGZV%252FUntitled%2520%2876%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7212776b-4eb7-4e88-9d05-f868542bb537&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6d3b77db&sv=2)

Improvements and bug fixes

*   Updated navigation in the presentation generator window. Custom instructions and presets now live together in the [Team Library](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/presets)
    .
    
*   Fixed an issue where some prompts would hit the character limit in [text to presentation](https://guide.plusdocs.com/plus-ai/generate-a-presentation/text-to-presentation)
     mode prematurely.
    
*   Fixed a bug where [text to presentation mode](https://guide.plusdocs.com/plus-ai/generate-a-presentation/text-to-presentation)
     would sometimes generate slides in English instead of the [original language](https://guide.plusdocs.com/plus-ai/languages)
    .
    
*   Fixed a bug in the Google Slides add-on that allowed you to submit an empty prompt (which unsurprisingly wouldn’t lead to a very good presentation.)
    
*   Fixed a couple of bugs with [custom themes](https://guide.plusdocs.com/plus-ai/custom-themes)
     that were preventing some users from generating presentations when using a custom theme with a logo.
    
*   Improved text fitting in Google Slides so there are fewer overflowing text boxes.
    
*   Added the ability to invite teammates directly within the Google Slides add-on.
    

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#september-2023)

September 2023


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#feature-text-to-presentation-mode)

Feature: Text to presentation mode

Text to presentation mode allows you to paste in a large amount of text, which Plus AI will summarize and repackage into a presentation. Especially useful for converting documents, articles, or other text-based content into slides. [Learn more.](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/upload-a-file)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252FRtLTGfAvUJOtWtz8GJaZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5390e225-16f8-4769-8240-265fbf74acd3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5780c8f&sv=2)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#feature-slide-by-slide-mode)

Feature: Slide by slide mode

Slide by slide mode lets you build a presentation one slide at a time. Instead of writing one prompt for the entire presentation, you can specify exactly what you want on each slide. If you'd like, you can also choose a specific layout for each slide. [Learn more.](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/generate-a-presentation/slide-by-slide)

![](https://guide.plusai.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3528250745-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F54nb5b7bqXPHgn40UzoV%252Fuploads%252Fs31EQkwr0kOmwZg5wgDv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd1e4993b-ef60-4df0-8ced-999dd02a5251&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=16f08d59&sv=2)

### 

[](https://guide.plusai.com/help/plus-ai-changelog#improvements-and-bug-fixes-7)

Improvements and bug fixes

*   Added support for rich text in text to presentation mode.
    
*   Added more slide designs with images. Tuned Plus AI to use more images when designing presentations.
    
*   Updated the Plus Unicorn theme. Now it works with [Insert](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/insert-a-single-slide)
     and [Rewrite](https://guide.plusai.com/ai-for-presentations/rewrite-slides)
     and is cloneable.
    
*   Various bug fixes and improvements to increase reliability of Plus AI.
